卸載怠速 (Unload-Idle)：在需求低谷時讓壓縮機空轉（不輸出氣體），比頻繁啟停對設備的損耗更小。

公式與計算 — 控制方式耗電比較

進氣節流 (Inlet Throttling)：
  0% 輸出 → 仍耗 ~70% 滿載電力
  有效調節範圍：50–60% 最大容量

變頻控制 (VSD)：
  輸出正比於轉速
  20% 輸出 → 約 20–30% 電力消耗
  （節能效果顯著）

生命週期成本 (Life Cycle Cost, LCC) 考量：
  VSD 初始成本高 + 節電收益
  vs. 節流閥 低初始成本 + 長期高電費

重點提示 Key Notes

控制系統的選擇直接影響廠務的年度能源帳單。製藥廠的壓縮空氣系統通常 24/7 運行，VSD 在需求波動大的廠區（如多批次 CDMO）節省的電費往往在 2–3 年內可回收設備投資差額。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您的廠區壓縮機使用哪種控制方式？在非生產時段（如夜間、週末），系統如何管理需求降低的情況？
  2. 為什麼說「排氣節流」是效率最差的控制方式，且在實務中幾乎不被採用？
4.5 Air Treatment & ISO 8573-1 Quality Classes — 空氣處理與品質等級

原文內容 Original Text

Treating compressed air to remove contaminants such as dirt (viable and non-viable particulate), lubricant, and water, may use equipment such as:

  • compressor aftercoolers
  • filters
  • separators
  • dryers
  • air receivers
  • traps
  • automatic drains

A commonly recognized standard is ISO 8573-1:2010 which identifies three classes of contaminants:

  1. particulate
  2. water
  3. oil/oil vapor

ISO 8573-1:2010 does not differentiate viable and non-viable particulates. Therefore, when using ISO 8573-1:2010 to define purity class of compressed air, further definition may be required in the User Requirements.

Quality Class Particulate 0.1–0.5 µm /m³ Particulate 0.5–1.0 µm /m³ Particulate 1.0–5.0 µm /m³ Pressure Dew Point (°C) Oil & Vapor (mg/m³)
0 As specified by user — more stringent than Class 1
1 ≤ 20,000 ≤ 400 ≤ 10 −70°C ≤ 0.01
2 ≤ 400,000 ≤ 6,000 ≤ 100 −40°C ≤ 0.1
3 — ≤ 90,000 ≤ 1,000 −20°C ≤ 1
4 — — ≤ 10,000 +3°C ≤ 5
5 — — ≤ 100,000 +7°C > 5
6 — — — +10°C > 5

Measurements relate to standard conditions of 20°C, 1 bar absolute pressure.

4.5.1 Air Inlet Filters

Air inlet filters protect compressors from atmospheric airborne particles. Air inlet filters do not determine final air quality. Provided the air quality will not compromise the compressor reliability, it may be more cost effective to treat the air downstream of the compressor.

4.5.2 Intercooler and Aftercoolers

Intercoolers and aftercoolers are heat exchangers designed to remove heat of compression, to improve system efficiency. Moisture separators following an intercooler or aftercooler separate liquids entrained in the air or gas.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

ISO 8573-1:2010 是壓縮空氣品質的國際標準，定義三類污染物的七個等級（Class 0–6）：

  • 微粒 (Particulate)：依顆粒大小與濃度分級
  • 水分 (Water)：以壓力露點 (Pressure Dew Point, PDP) 表示
  • 油/油霧 (Oil & Vapor)：以 mg/m³ 表示

重要限制：ISO 8573-1 不區分活性（有微生物）與非活性微粒。製藥廠必須在 URS（使用者需求規格）中額外定義微生物限度。

重點提示 Key Notes — 製藥廠的品質目標

製藥製程空氣通常目標 ISO Class 1–2（油含量 ≤ 0.01–0.1 mg/m³），並搭配微生物規格（如 <1 CFU/m³ 或滅菌級 0.2 µm 過濾後無菌）。

Class 0 表示「用戶自訂、比 Class 1 更嚴格」，適用於最高品質要求的場合（如直接接觸無菌產品的壓縮空氣）。

比喻說明 Analogy

ISO 8573 的品質等級就像飲用水標準：Class 6 是工業冷卻水（能用就行），Class 1 是瓶裝礦泉水，Class 0 是注射用水級別。你的製程需要哪個等級，取決於空氣與產品的接觸程度——越靠近產品，要求越嚴格。

實務應用 Practical Application

CDMO 無菌充填廠的典型設計：

  • 隔離器加壓用壓縮空氣 → ISO Class 1 + 微生物 0 CFU（終端 0.2 µm 滅菌級過濾）
  • 塞子振動碗驅動空氣 → ISO Class 2 + 微生物管控
  • 氣動閥驅動 → ISO Class 3–4（儀器空氣）
  • 一般設備冷卻 → ISO Class 4–5
4.6 Dryers — 乾燥機類型比較

原文內容 Original Text

Once air leaves an aftercooler and moisture separator, its moisture content should have been reduced significantly; however, it may still be saturated. The temperature at which this moisture condenses is called the dewpoint. The dewpoint may be measured at line pressure or at atmospheric pressure.

Dryers are usually rated on pressure dewpoint. Dryer design should anticipate worst case operating condition based on the maximum allowable dewpoint. Types of dryers include:

  1. regenerative-desiccant dryer
  2. heat-of-compression dryer
  3. refrigerant dryer

4.6.1 Regenerative-Desiccant Dryers

Regenerative-desiccant dryers normally use a porous desiccant that adsorbs moisture. Desiccants include: silica gel, activated alumina, molecular sieves.

Normally, the desiccant resides in a twin tower. Compressed air to be dried flows through one tower, while the desiccant in the other is being regenerated. There are three types:

  1. Heatless dryer: requires about 15% of the dryer's capacity to be used for purge air, but normally has lowest initial cost.
  2. Heated dryer: reduces purge to 7 or 8%, but may cost more than a heatless dryer.
  3. Blower purge dryer: can reduce purge to 0 to 2%, but may cost more than a heated dryer.

Regenerative-desiccant-type dryers are commonly used in pharmaceutical manufacturing applications for process air, as they have a dewpoint rating more than 70°F (21°C) lower than refrigerant dryers (-40°F / -40°C dewpoint at standard inlet conditions).

4.6.2 Heat-of-Compression Dryers

Heat-of-compression dryers are regenerative desiccant dryers that use the heat generated during compression to achieve desiccant regeneration. They represent an efficient means for drying to −40°F (−40°C) dewpoint using either no or only small amounts of purge air for regeneration. Both require hot air from lubricant free rotary or centrifugal compressors.

Single-Vessel: A rotating desiccant drum directs air into two separate air streams. Where load is variable, so is the dewpoint. Heat-of-compression dryers are unlikely to provide −40°F (−40°C) constant dewpoint.

Twin-Tower: This dryer can be designed for constant dewpoint with varying loads. It has low to no purge air and repeatable dewpoint.

4.6.3 Refrigerant Dryers

Refrigerant dryers have low initial and operating costs, but are not frequently used in pharmaceutical applications for process air, as they usually require a much lower dewpoint. Refrigerated dryers provide a dewpoint in the 38°F to 50°F (3°C to 10°C) range.

Where process air system generation is combined with instrument air systems, it would not be unusual to use a refrigerated air dryer for the main generation system and a smaller desiccant dryer for the process air branch requirements.

Technology Purge Air Achievable Dewpoint
Heatless Desiccant 15% −40°F to −100°F
Externally Heated Desiccant 7–8% −40°F to −100°F
Blower Purge Desiccant 0–3% −40°F
Heat of Compression – Drum 0% 0 to −20°F
Heat of Compression – Twin Tower 0–2% < −20°F
Refrigerant Dryer N/A +38°F to +50°F (3–10°C)

Table 4.2: Comparison of Dryer Technologies

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

露點 (Dew Point)：空氣中的水蒸氣在某溫度下開始凝結為液態水——這個溫度即為露點。露點越低，代表空氣越乾燥。

壓力露點 (Pressure Dew Point, PDP)：在配管工作壓力下測量的露點，是壓縮空氣系統的標準規格指標。

吸附式再生乾燥機 (Regenerative Desiccant Dryer)：雙塔設計，一塔吸附除濕，另一塔同時進行再生（加熱驅出水分）。製藥廠首選。

冷凍式乾燥機 (Refrigerant Dryer)：以冷媒冷卻空氣使水蒸氣冷凝排出，露點約 +3 至 +10°C，初期成本低但露點不夠低，不適合大多數製藥製程空氣用途。

比喻說明 Analogy

冷凍式乾燥機就像冰箱裡的除濕盒——能讓空氣變乾一點，但到冬天（低溫環境）就沒效了。吸附式乾燥機則像矽膠乾燥劑包——不管什麼溫度都能持續吸濕，而且可以加熱再生重複使用。製藥廠需要全年穩定的超低露點，吸附式因此成為首選。

重點提示 Key Notes — 吹掃損耗

無加熱型吸附乾燥機 (Heatless) 需要消耗 15% 的乾燥空氣來吹掃再生另一塔。對壓縮空氣系統而言，這 15% 就是白白損失的能源。

外加熱型可減至 7–8%，鼓風吹掃型減至 0–2%，但設備成本逐步上升。選型時需做生命週期成本 (LCC) 分析，而非只看初始設備報價。

熱壓縮式 (Heat-of-Compression) 單容器型的露點會隨負荷變化而漂移——不適合需要穩定露點的 GMP 製程。應優先選用雙塔型以獲得穩定露點。

公式與計算 — 吹掃損耗對系統容量的影響

系統設計壓縮機容量必須涵蓋吹掃損耗：

若製程需求 = 1,000 cfm 乾燥空氣
使用無加熱型乾燥機（15% 吹掃）：

壓縮機需輸出 = 1,000 / (1 - 0.15)
             = 1,000 / 0.85
             ≈ 1,176 cfm 總輸出

→ 多設計 17.6% 的壓縮機容量來補償吹掃損耗

換用鼓風吹掃型（2% 吹掃）：
壓縮機需輸出 = 1,000 / 0.98 ≈ 1,020 cfm
→ 節省顯著！

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您廠目前的製程空氣系統使用哪種乾燥機？其壓力露點規格為何？是否能達到 USP <1> 或 EP 對壓縮空氣的要求？
  2. 若儀器空氣與製程空氣共用同一套主系統，且主系統裝的是冷凍式乾燥機，製程空氣分支應如何補充處理？
4.7 Compressed Air Filters — 壓縮空氣過濾器

原文內容 Original Text

Compressed air filters downstream of the air compressor are normally required for the removal of contaminants. Types of filter available include:

  • particulate filters to remove solid particles
  • coalescing filters to remove hydrocarbon droplets, moisture droplets, and particulates
  • adsorbent filters to remove hydrocarbon vapors and other aromatics (odors and tastes)

A particulate filter may be recommended after a desiccant-type dryer to remove desiccant dust. A coalescing-type filter may be recommended before a desiccant-type dryer to prevent fouling of the desiccant bed if a lubricant injected compressor is used upstream.

Filter grades of 0.45 µm or 0.2 µm may be employed at POUs (Point of Use).

When reviewing filters for their applicability, particle size removal ratings (e.g., 0.2 µm) and the filter efficiency rating (e.g., 99.97% efficient) should be reviewed. These ratings are normally based on defined inlet conditions, usually 70°F (21°C) at 100 psig.

A typical sequence of filters for a system is:

  1. Particulate Filter: typically 1 µm to 3 µm for removing rust, pipe scale, metal oxides, and desiccant particles
  2. High Temperature Particulate Filter: Temperature spikes can occur when using a heated desiccant dryer. Similar ratings to standard particulates apply, but can withstand higher operating temperatures to 350°F to 450°F (176.7°C to 232.2°C).
  3. Coalescing Filters: Liquid droplet removal capacity is typically 0.001 ppm by weight and aerosol size rated at 0.01 µm.
  4. Final Filter: A 0.2 µm liquid rated cartridge filter (down to 0.003 µm absolute rated for particles in gases) may be used as a final filter to obtain "sterile grade" compressed air. These filter cartridges are typically sanitary style to minimize the risk of bypass and incorporate a hydrophobic non-volatile membrane as the filter media.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

過濾器種類三大類：

  • 微粒過濾器 (Particulate Filter)：去除固態微粒（鐵鏽、管垢、吸附劑粉塵），通常 1–3 µm 評級。
  • 聚結過濾器 (Coalescing Filter)：讓細小油霧或水霧液滴聚合成大液滴後流出。聚結效率可達 0.01 µm 液霧。
  • 吸附過濾器 (Adsorbent/Activated Carbon Filter)：去除油蒸氣等氣態碳氫化合物，通常以活性碳為介質。

使用點過濾器 (POU Filter)：0.2 µm 疏水性膜過濾器，用於最終滅菌級壓縮空氣，防止微生物穿透。

比喻說明 Analogy

壓縮空氣過濾鏈路就像城市自來水系統：先是粗濾網擋掉大顆粒，再是沉澱池去除懸浮物，再是活性碳濾除異味，最後才是 0.2 µm 超濾膜確保飲用安全。每一層都有它的任務，缺一不可，順序也不能錯。

重點提示 Key Notes

加熱型吸附乾燥機在塔切換瞬間，會有短暫的溫度峰值（Heat Spike）。普通聚結過濾器可能因高溫而失效，必須在此位置使用高溫型微粒過濾器（耐 176–232°C）。

最終 0.2 µm 滅菌級過濾器的設計要點：使用衛生型殼體以防止旁路；濾膜材質必須為疏水性（不吸水），確保壓縮空氣通暢流過而水不會被攔截造成壓降過大。

實務應用 Practical Application

典型 CDMO 無菌充填線的壓縮空氣過濾配置（由上游到使用點）：

  1. 壓縮機出口 → 聚結預過濾（去除油霧，保護吸附乾燥機）
  2. 吸附乾燥機出口 → 1–3 µm 微粒過濾（去除吸附劑粉塵）
  3. 分配管網入口 → 活性碳吸附過濾（去除殘留碳氫蒸氣）
  4. 使用點 (POU) → 0.2 µm 疏水性滅菌級過濾（無菌空氣進入填充區）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若廠區使用無油壓縮機，是否仍需要聚結過濾器？為什麼？（提示：考慮配管中的潤滑脂污染可能性）
  2. 0.2 µm 過濾器的使用完整性測試 (Integrity Test) 應在什麼時機進行？（參照 EU GMP Annex 1 對過濾器管理的要求）
4.8 Air Receivers — 空氣儲槽

原文內容 Original Text

Receivers can be used to provide surge capacity to meet peak process needs and minimize changes in system pressure during periods of peak demand.

Compressed air systems require a receiver. When demand peaks are short and limited (usually less than 60 to 90 seconds), a large air receiver may allow a smaller air compressor to be specified. Additional benefits include the:

  • improved system reliability, as the load cycles on the compressor are reduced
  • increased efficiency, as the likelihood of another compressor starting is minimized

A desiccant dryer's purge can be the temporary push to peak demand. Given the cyclical nature of purge, it creates a temporary artificial demand on the compressor for a brief period but can be invisible to the compressor controls with a wet air receiver (i.e., an air receiver placed before a purge type desiccant dryer).

A receiver placed downstream of air treatment equipment can be used to manage pressure variation in a distribution system.

"A rule of thumb used for sizing a receiver is to use a unit with a capacity of 6 to 10 times the compressor peak capacity (free air delivered/second)."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

溼空氣儲槽 (Wet Receiver)：位於壓縮機與乾燥機之間，緩衝乾燥機再生吹掃造成的瞬間壓降，讓壓縮機「看不見」吹掃需求，避免頻繁啟動。

乾空氣儲槽 (Dry Receiver)：位於乾燥機下游，作為緩衝儲能，穩定配管網路的壓力波動，應對短時間的高峰需求。

電容量 (Capacitance)：本文用這個物理學類比描述儲槽的「緩衝能量」——就像電容在電路中平滑電壓波動。

公式與計算 — 儲槽尺寸估算

儲槽選型經驗法則：
  容積 = 6–10 × 壓縮機峰值輸出 (FAD/秒)

範例：
  壓縮機輸出 = 50 cfm = 0.83 cf/s
  建議儲槽容積 = 6 × 0.83 至 10 × 0.83
               = 5 至 8.3 立方英尺 (cf)
               ≈ 140 至 235 公升

注意：
  高峰需求超過 60–90 秒 → 需要更大儲槽
  或升級更大壓縮機容量

重點提示 Key Notes

空氣儲槽是壓力容器，受各國法規管制（美國 ASME Boiler & Pressure Vessel Code，歐洲 PED）。必須定期進行檢驗（壓力測試、外觀檢查）並納入廠務保養計畫。

儲槽底部會積累冷凝水（因空氣在儲存中降溫），必須設置適當的排放機制（traps / drains），否則水分會進入下游系統。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼吸附乾燥機的再生吹掃會對壓縮機造成「人為的瞬間需求峰值」？溼空氣儲槽如何解決這個問題？
  2. 您廠的壓縮空氣儲槽上次法規要求的壓力容器檢驗是何時？是否有完整紀錄？
4.9 Traps and Drains — 冷凝液疏水閥與排水

原文內容 Original Text

Traps or drains allow the removal of condensate from the compressed air system to protect the equipment being supplied by the system from the effects of a non-compressible fluid. Automatic condensate traps are used to conserve energy by preventing the loss of air through open petcocks and valves.

Methods to drain condensate include:

  1. mechanical traps
  2. solenoid actuated drain valves
  3. zero air-loss traps with reservoirs
  4. manual

4.9.1 Mechanical Traps

These are usually float-type mechanical traps with inverted buckets as a secondary design feature. Float-type traps are designed to open only as increasing condensate raises the water level and consequently, a float. Before the water is fully evacuated, the float reseals the trap, to prevent waste of air.

These traps can easily be blocked by buildup of particulate in the condensate. The inspection and maintenance of these traps should be incorporated into a maintenance program.

4.9.2 Solenoid Actuated Drain Valves

Solenoid-actuated drain valves are electrically operated and employ a timed sequence for opening and closing. Concerns include:

  • The open interval duration may be inadequate to evacuate all condensate.
  • The closed interval may be too long creating a back up of condensate into the compression stages.

The settings on these units should be revised depending on seasonal variation in outside air supplied to a system.

4.9.3 Zero-Air-Loss Traps with Reservoirs

Zero-air-loss traps can improve efficiency of a compressed air system. Types include:

  1. solenoid actuated with level sensor
  2. pneumatically actuated air cylinder, which opens a ball valve through a linkage to expel the condensate in the reservoir to the low-level point

Zero-air-loss traps combine the efficiency of no air loss and reduced maintenance with larger orifices, typically preventing the build-up of particulate in the trap. Strainers are recommended for all traps to prevent the likelihood of sediment blocking the passage of condensate.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

冷凝液 (Condensate)：壓縮空氣降溫後析出的液態水（可能含有油分），必須定期排放，否則進入設備會造成腐蝕、微生物滋生，甚至損壞氣動元件（液體不可壓縮）。

零氣損疏水閥 (Zero Air-Loss Trap)：最高效的排水方式——先將冷凝液蓄積在小型儲存腔，達到液位後才開閥排放，不讓壓縮空氣同時逸出。

比喻說明 Analogy

浮球式疏水閥就像廁所的浮球水箱：水位高時開閥排放，水排完浮球下降關閥。問題是若浮球機構裡積了雜質，就可能卡死不動作。電磁閥式定時排水則像定時澆花器——不管有沒有水都按時開關，在夏天（空氣含水量高）可能不夠用，冬天則可能浪費大量空氣。

重點提示 Key Notes

電磁閥式疏水閥的定時設定需要隨季節調整！台灣夏季濕度高，空氣含水量是冬季的 3–5 倍，冷凝液生成量大幅增加。固定不變的開閥間隔可能導致冷凝液滿溢，或者白白放掉大量壓縮空氣。建議納入每季廠務維保確認項目。

油水混合的冷凝液屬工業廢水，不能直接排入水溝——必須經過油水分離系統處理，這是環保法規的要求，也是稽查重點之一。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果您廠使用電磁閥式疏水閥，應如何設計確認程序，確保在不同季節條件下冷凝液都能被有效排除？
  2. 所有疏水閥前建議加裝過濾網 (Strainer)，這解決了什麼問題？與不加過濾網相比，維護頻率會如何變化？
4.10 Designing for Redundancy — 備援設計（N+1 策略）

原文內容 Original Text

The design of a compressed air system should consider the implications of loss of supply to the process. The N+1 redundancy strategy — where N is the number of compressors required to meet the demand, plus one standby unit — is a common approach to ensure continuity of supply.

Key redundancy design considerations include:

  • Standby compressors should be capable of being brought online automatically or with minimal manual intervention in the event of a primary compressor failure.
  • Redundancy of filters or dryer with transfer valves may be necessary to allow maintenance to be performed safely while a system is kept operational.
  • Control systems should be configured to monitor system pressure and automatically switch to standby equipment when the primary unit fails or drops below a set pressure threshold.
  • Planned maintenance of one compressor should be possible without interrupting the supply to the process (i.e., the remaining compressors can carry the full process load).

The level of redundancy should be proportional to the criticality of the application. For critical pharmaceutical manufacturing processes where loss of compressed air supply could lead to batch loss, equipment damage, or patient safety risk, a higher level of redundancy is justified.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

N+1 備援策略：N 台壓縮機足夠應付正常需求，額外再加 1 台備用機。若任一台故障或進行維護，其餘機台仍可滿足完整製程需求。

類似邏輯也應用於：乾燥機（並聯雙套，帶切換閥）、主要過濾器（並聯旁通設計）。

比喻說明 Analogy

N+1 就像飛機的雙引擎設計——平常兩台引擎各出一半力，一台故障時另一台能獨力維持飛行。製藥廠的壓縮空氣也是這樣：不能為了省錢買單台大機，一旦故障整個製程停擺，那批次損失的代價往往比備援設備更貴。

公式與計算 — 備援投資的 ROI 分析

備援壓縮機成本：$150,000–300,000 USD（典型）

壓縮空氣故障造成的批次損失：
  無菌充填批次 × 損失風險（批均值）
  = 例如：2批 × $500,000/批 = $1,000,000

年化故障機率（未備援）：
  假設 MTBF = 5年 → 故障機率 20%/年

預期年損失 = $1,000,000 × 20% = $200,000/年

投資回收期 ≈ $250,000 / $200,000 ≈ 1.25 年

結論：備援壓縮機通常 1–2 年內回收投資

重點提示 Key Notes — CDMO 的備援邏輯

對 CDMO 而言，壓縮空氣故障的影響不只是一批產品，而是：

  • 隔離器失壓 → 無菌環境立即失效 → 整條線需要重新確認
  • 塞子振動碗停止 → 充填線中斷 → 部分充填批次可能需廢棄
  • 氣動門/閥無法動作 → 人員無法安全進出生產區
  • 客戶關係損失 → CDMO 的聲譽和合約續簽

這些連鎖影響讓 N+1 備援的商業論據非常清晰——這不只是技術問題，而是 CDMO 業務連續性 (Business Continuity) 的核心保障。

實務應用 Practical Application

建議操作：為您廠的壓縮空氣系統繪製一份「失效模式地圖」：

  1. 列出所有依賴壓縮空氣的關鍵設備（隔離器、充填機、氣動閥等）
  2. 評估各設備失去壓縮空氣後的影響程度（批次損失、安全風險、合規風險）
  3. 對最高風險節點，確認是否有足夠的備援（N+1、緊急氮氣備援、儲槽緩衝時間）
  4. 在變更管理 (Change Control) 中，記錄備援設計的合理性依據

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 您廠的壓縮空氣系統目前是 N+1 還是 N 配置？如果是 N，歷史上是否發生過因壓縮機故障導致生產中斷的事件？
  2. 備援壓縮機的「自動切換」功能需要定期驗證（如 PM 測試）。您廠的驗證頻率和測試程序是否已文件化？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • 系統架構：壓縮空氣系統分供給側（壓縮機＋處理設備）與需求側（配管＋POU），需作為整體系統設計，而非各自獨立考量。
  • 無油壓縮機：製藥製程空氣的行業標準。油潤式壓縮機出口含 2–5 ppm 油分，即使加裝聚結過濾器仍有殘留風險，不適合 product-contact 應用。
  • 乾燥機選型：吸附式再生乾燥機可達 −40°C 以下壓力露點，是製藥製程空氣的首選；冷凍式僅能達 +3 至 +10°C，適用於儀器空氣。
  • 過濾鏈路：從 1–3 µm 粗濾到最終 0.2 µm 疏水性滅菌級過濾，每一層都有其不可替代的角色；溫度峰值位置需使用高溫型過濾器。
  • 儲槽功能：溼空氣儲槽緩衝乾燥機吹掃需求，乾空氣儲槽穩定配管壓力；選型以壓縮機峰值容量的 6–10 倍為參考。
  • 冷凝液管理：零氣損疏水閥效率最高；電磁閥式需隨季節調整設定；油水冷凝液須經油水分離後才能排放。
  • N+1 備援：對 CDMO 而言，壓縮空氣故障的連鎖損失（批次報廢、隔離器失壓、客戶信任）通常遠超備援設備的投資成本，備援是商業連續性的核心保障。
3

Chapter 3: Distribution Systems (Ch 5)

配送系統設計 | p53-p68

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases | p53–p68
ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases

本章學習目標

  • 理解環形主管（ring main）與單向配送（one-way distribution）兩種架構的設計邏輯與GMP優劣比較
  • 掌握非回流閥（non-return valve）防止逆流污染的原理及安裝規範，理解其在無菌產品系統中的法規必要性
  • 了解製程氣體過濾系統的完整層次：從源頭預過濾到使用點（POU）0.2 µm滅菌級過濾，以及三種完整性測試方法
  • 比較各種管路材質（不鏽鋼、銅、塑膠、碳鋼）的特性、適用情境與GxP限制，並能在CDMO現場做出有據可查的材質選擇決策
5.1 Concepts — 配送系統設計基本概念

原文內容 Original Text

The initial design of distribution systems for process gases should match the available gas quality and supply method to the end user specifications. This forms the basis for the design, and should provide detail on the:

  • level of clean-up required for a gas prior to use
  • the pressure control and management of the supply and delivery systems

Delivery of supplies of a gas at the required specification should be consistent. The capabilities of both internal (e.g., compressed air or nitrogen) and external (e.g., bottled or bulk gases) supplies should be considered.

A supplier audit may be required for external suppliers. A Certificate of Analysis (CoA) should ensure that a gas is of the required specification. Equipment used to provide the information for the CoA should be appropriately maintained and calibrated.

Supplies of internally manufactured gases (e.g., compressed air or nitrogen) should be considered in the same way as external supplies, including:

  • assessment of quality of supply
  • management and reporting of quality of supply
  • measurement and reporting of expected contaminants (e.g., oil carryover from a compressed air system)

5.1.1 Risk Assessment

The design process should include a risk assessment to ensure that the proposed design is fit for purpose. The assessment should consider potential systems failures and ensure that the controls in place are adequate to mitigate risks to product quality or patient safety.

Gas suppliers may have technical support staff that can assist during the risk assessment and system design phase of a project.

Depending on the pharmaceutical application, the environment in which the gas lines are run, and the quality of gas supplied, some aspects of industrial gas supply may not be required. These requirements should be considered during a risk assessment, e.g.:

  • Gases distributed for pharmaceutical applications are usually dry and of a high quality and may not require distribution systems to be drainable; pipe line fall, drop legs, and drain traps may not be needed.
  • Where a distribution system is clean, with a clean gas being distributed, having gas point take-offs at the top of a pipeline may not be required.

A risk assessment should also consider:

  • How operations are made aware that there is sufficient connected capacity to undertake a batch or process (e.g., use of monitoring systems and back-up supplies for critical processes)
  • Whether automatic changeover for finite supply applications (bulk or cylinders) is required, or if a suitable low pressure/low level warning system is sufficient
  • For flammable, toxic, or corrosive gases: control of discharge from regulators and lines during cylinder changeover, line disconnection, or in the event of line or regulator failure
  • Effects on staff from exposure to a gas in general operation and during potential failure modes (e.g., oxygen exclusion, flammability, static build-up, chemical reaction)
  • High concentration of all gases (including inert) should be considered to present a risk to personnel

Document all steps as part of the design risk assessment.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

配送系統設計 (Distribution System Design): 不是選一條管路接到設備就完成了。設計的起點是「使用端規格書（end user specification）」——你的製程需要多純的氣體、多大的流量、多少壓力，設計才從這裡往回推。

CoA — Certificate of Analysis（分析證明書）: 每批次/每桶外購氣體的品質保證文件。ISPE強調：外購氣體供應商等同原料供應商，需要供應商稽核（supplier audit）、CoA審查，以及設備的校驗記錄。這在FDA查廠時必查。

內部製造氣體的盲區: 許多CDMO習慣把壓縮空氣視為「公用設施」而非「原料」，但ISPE明確要求：自製氣體（compressed air、nitrogen）需要與外購氣體完全相同的品質管理機制，包括污染物報告（如油份攜帶）。

比喻說明 Analogy

把製程氣體配送系統想像成醫院的供氧管路。醫院不會隨便拉一條塑膠管就接到手術室的氧氣口——它需要材質驗證、壓力計算、備援系統、以及每個接頭的防回流設計。你的藥廠氣體配送系統也是如此：病人安全（= 產品品質）就建立在這套設計的嚴謹程度上。

重點提示 Key Notes

風險評估（risk assessment）是整個第5章的核心邏輯主軸。ISPE不規定你一定要做環形管路、一定要裝多少過濾器——它要求你透過風險評估來決定哪些工業標準做法在GMP環境中可以免除，哪些必須保留。這種「基於風險的彈性」正是現代法規的精神，也是你在工程設計時最重要的文件化工具。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的廠區自製壓縮空氣目前有沒有CoA制度？如果沒有，這在法規上代表什麼風險？
  2. 為什麼ISPE說藥廠氣體通常「不需要設計排水斜度（pipe line fall）」？這與工業壓縮空氣系統的差異何在？
5.1.2 Basic System Design Concepts — 基本系統設計概念

原文內容 Original Text

Process take-off requirements should be understood to allow sizing of a distribution system. The rate of gas usage and pressure required at critical points in the process should be quantified. These critical points should include periods of peak take-off of gas. The distribution system should be sized to maintain an adequate supply at critical points.

Averages should not be used, even where there is variable take-off of gas. (Experienced designers may use a system utilization factor.)

Basic system design concepts include:

  • one way distribution system
  • high demand use points
  • ring main
  • splitting systems
  • use of a non-return valve/receiver to split systems
  • line sizing
  • routing

5.1.2.1 One Way Distribution System

The simplest distribution system design comprises a single pipeline feeding each POU (point of use). For a small number of widely spaced delivery points, a one way distribution system from a gas source may represent the lowest initial cost at installation. The pipeline should be sized to accommodate peak usage.

Where the highest gas consumption POUs are positioned nearest the gas supply, it may be possible to reduce the size of the pipeline to POUs further along the system. Intermediate receiving vessels may be used to reduce the effects of usage variability or supply line size. They may be placed in the main branch or on critical POUs and used where the:

  • highest gas consumption POUs cannot be sited nearest the gas supply
  • size of pipeline to provide peak loads is excessive
  • demand varies significantly

Intermediate receiving vessels can buffer the output to specific POUs (e.g., nitrogen inertion of large API reactor systems). Consideration should be given to providing non-return valves at intermediate receiving vessels to ensure that the main pipeline is not back fed if the main pipeline pressure dips below the receiver pressure at high demand periods.

5.1.2.2 Ring Main

A ring main comprises two feed sources. The ring main concept is considered a more robust distribution design when compared to a one way design, as:

  • The system will self balance due to the two feed sources of the ring main allowing line size to be optimized. Points at the extreme of the ring may be susceptible to pressure drops but these will be reduced.
  • A considered design and placement of isolation valves will allow the line to be serviced, modified, or repaired without shutting down the complete ring and associated POUs.
  • The ring main itself provides a level of receiver capacity which may be sufficient to buffer high demand, reducing the need for intermediate receiving vessels.
  • The system allows addition of multiple gas sources (e.g., multiple air compressors) in different locations throughout the site, enhancing the redundancy of the system.

A ring main system can provide a cost effective solution relative to a one way distribution line, particularly where cost analysis includes allowances for foreseeable future growth.

5.1.2.3 High Demand Points of Use

Where there are high demand POUs, it may be more economic to provide gas from a local receiving vessel using a smaller distribution system pipeline size at a higher supply pressure. Consideration should be given to over-sizing the distribution pipe locally to the POU to provide a "local receiver."

Consideration should be given to providing non-return valves at intermediate receiving vessels to ensure that the main pipeline is not back fed particularly where several buffering receivers are attached to one supply. Pressure and flow regulation should be considered in the distribution system design.

5.1.2.4 Splitting Systems

Requirements of relevant GMP codes (e.g., system design and documentation, validation processes, ongoing maintenance, calibration quality monitoring, and formal monitoring of the system output quality) add to the installation and operating costs of GMP gas distribution systems.

Where end-user specifications allow, it may be feasible to split a system into non-GMP and GMP sub-systems. This may be particularly beneficial in locations where there is a large site gas distribution system, with only a limited part of the system used for GMP purposes. A non-GMP system can be used to feed a GMP system, providing that the GMP system is adequately monitored and controlled.

The risk assessment associated with a split system should consider how the integrity, purity, and quality of the GMP take-off points is maintained under all scenarios. Redundancy in filtration and back flow prevention may be required.

5.1.2.5 Sizing of Pipes

Pipe size can be based on either a calculated design maximum use or the total connected load multiplied by a diversity factor. Typical figures used are 6–9 m/s (18–27 ft/sec) velocity, or 3–5 psi (0.3 to 0.4 bar) allowable pressure drop, depending on conditions. Filter pressure drops should be considered in calculations.

The greater the pressure drop, the greater the minimum system supply pressure needs to be. As pressure increases, the energy requirement for the compressor (or cost of bulk gas) increases following a square law — so small differences have a significant effect on energy consumption.

5.1.2.6 Routing

The siting of pipes should facilitate regular inspection and servicing of valves. Annual checks for leaks may be conducted as part of GEP using techniques such as ultrasonic leak detection. Statutory periodic inspections may be required for high pressure equipment in some geographical regions.

Where a process gas has a dewpoint near the local environmental limits, pipes should be insulated or sited where they do not cause internal or external condensation.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：Ring Main vs. One-Way 的設計哲學

單向配送 (One-Way Distribution): 像一條單車道的馬路——起點到終點，氣體只有一條路走。好處是管路簡單、成本低；壞處是終端使用點的壓力會隨距離和需求波動而不穩定，且任何一段管路維修就影響所有下游用點。

環形主管 (Ring Main): 像城市的環狀公路——氣體可以從左邊或右邊同時進入任何一個出口，壓力自動趨於平衡。這是藥廠大型生產線的首選，特別是當未來有擴產計畫時。

比喻說明 Analogy

Ring main就像台北的捷運環狀線。任何一個站發生問題，乘客可以繞另一半圓繼續走。相對地，單向系統就像只有一條路的公路——一旦中斷，所有車都堵死了。對於24小時連續生產的CDMO廠，「任何單點故障不影響全線生產」這個特性值多少錢，就是ring main設計費用的正當化基礎。

公式與計算 Pipe Sizing Reference

管路尺寸設計兩種方法：

方法一：最大流速法
  典型流速上限：6–9 m/s（18–27 ft/sec）
  超過此速度 → 壓降急增 + 噪音 + 管件磨損加速

方法二：允許壓降法
  允許壓降：3–5 psi（0.3–0.4 bar）全程
  壓降增加 → 需提高供氣壓力
  壓力增加遵循平方律（square law）：
  能耗 ∝ P²
  → 供氣壓力提高10%，能耗約增加21%

注意事項：
  過濾器壓降（clean + dirty）必須納入計算
  峰值需求（peak load）而非平均值作為設計基準

重點提示：非GMP系統餵入GMP系統的風險

5.1.2.4的「系統分割」是很多大型藥廠實際採用的做法：讓工廠原有的大型工業壓縮空氣系統供氣給整廠，然後在進入GMP區前設一套「哨兵過濾組（policing filter set）」和非回流閥，把GMP段獨立出來。

這個設計的關鍵在於：GMP段的品質必須能在「工業段品質惡化」的情況下依然受控。這意味著GMP段需要自己的監測、自己的記錄，以及足夠的冗餘過濾。

實務應用 CDMO Scenario

在CDMO的多客戶環境中，ring main設計特別重要。不同客戶的製程可能在同一天使用不同量的氮氣或壓縮空氣。Ring main的「自平衡」特性讓高用量製程不會影響其他區域的壓力穩定性。同時，ring main上設置足夠的隔離閥（isolation valves），使工程師可以在不停止全廠生產的情況下維護任何一段管路——這正是FDA查廠時關注的「可維護性（maintainability）」設計要素。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的廠區計畫5年後新增一條無菌充填線，現在設計氣體配送系統時應選擇ring main還是one-way？理由是什麼？
  2. 為什麼管路設計不能用平均流量，而必須用峰值流量？用一個實際生產情境說明。
  3. 「壓降與壓力成平方律關係」對日常運轉成本有什麼實際意義？
5.2 Non-Return or Check Valves — 非回流閥／止回閥

原文內容 Original Text

There are several types of non-return valves. For process gases, the spring loaded wafer check valve, using an elastomeric seal for the wafer, allows a gas tight shut off and rapid action whichever way up the valve is mounted.

Non-return valves should be suitable for both the gas supply side and for likely contaminants from the process side.

For GMP systems, cross contamination can be considered a critical risk. Risk assessments performed during the design of a process gas system should investigate potential consequences of reverse flow under normal and system failure modes. Where a potential risk is identified, backflow prevention and non-return valves may be required.

Non-return valves should be fitted as closely as possible to POUs to reduce potential contamination in the supply line. Where there is a potential for cross contamination, cleaning and servicing of non-return valves should ensure that non-return valves remain functional. Redundancy may be required for high risk critical processes.

Where the function of a non-return valve is considered critical (as a process or a safety requirement), the systems design should facilitate testing of the non-return valve. This may be achieved either by making removal of the non-return valve easy, or by the installation of test ports on either side of the non-return valve and isolating valves in the line either side of the non-return valve.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

非回流閥 / 止回閥 (Non-Return Valve / Check Valve): 氣體只能向一個方向流動的閥件。對無菌藥品來說，這是防止「產品污染物沿氣體管路逆流回供氣系統」的最後一道實體屏障。

彈簧式晶片止回閥 (Spring-Loaded Wafer Check Valve): ISPE推薦的製程氣體類型。其特點是：彈性密封材質確保氣密性、彈簧確保快速關閉、設計不依賴重力故可任意角度安裝。這三個特性在複雜管路佈局中非常實用。

測試口 (Test Ports): 安裝在非回流閥兩側，讓維護人員可以在不拆閥的情況下進行功能驗證。這是高風險製程的必要設計——如果你的非回流閥是「關鍵功能」，就必須能夠被測試。

重點提示：逆流污染的實際場景

想像一個凍乾機（lyophilizer）在充填氮氣進行頭空間保護時，如果下游閥件失效，產品蒸汽（含有機物或微生物）可能順著氮氣管路逆流進入整個供氣系統，污染後續批次的所有頭空間保護用氣。這正是為什麼ISPE要求非回流閥「盡可能靠近POU安裝」——逆流行進的距離越短，潛在污染範圍越小。

FDA 21 CFR Part 211對製藥用公用設施的汙染防制有明確要求，非回流閥的設計和驗證記錄在查廠時是必查項目。

比喻說明 Analogy

非回流閥就像浴室排水管的P型彎管（存水彎）——它讓水只能向一個方向走，防止下水道的廢氣逆流進浴室。在藥廠氣體系統中，它防止的不是臭氣，而是可能危及藥品品質的微生物或有機污染物。而「需要測試口」的邏輯也很直觀：如果你家的P型彎管是安全關鍵設施，你應該能在不拆管的情況下測試它還有沒有在正常工作。

實務應用 CDMO Inspection Perspective

FDA查廠時，查察官對氣體系統非回流閥的關注點：

  • 安裝位置：是否緊鄰POU，而非安裝在遠端主管上？
  • 材質兼容性：閥體密封材料是否與氣體及可能的製程側污染物兼容？
  • 驗證記錄：非回流閥的功能是否有定期測試？測試方法、頻率、驗收標準是否記錄在SOP中？
  • 冗餘設計：高風險製程（如直接產品接觸氣體）是否有雙重非回流閥或其他備援？

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在什麼情況下單一非回流閥不夠，需要冗餘設計（redundancy）？
  2. 非回流閥安裝在主管而非POU附近，會帶來什麼風險？
5.3 Pressure Reducing Valves — 減壓閥

原文內容 Original Text

Pressure reducing valves should be selected so that the normal operating range is in the mid-point of the valve capabilities. Operating near the extremes of the valve capabilities may give less consistent results.

Materials of construction should be selected based on the properties of the gas being supplied and anticipated processes, e.g.:

  1. To extend the operating life of the valve where highly corrosive gases (e.g., hydrogen chloride gas) or processes occur, purging tees may be used to allow the pressure reducing valve to be purged after use with a suitable purging gas. For example, for hydrogen chloride gas, the purging gas could be dry nitrogen.
  2. For sterile operations where the gas may come into direct contact with the product (e.g., purging/headspace gas in a freeze drying process), the materials of construction and finish can be critical.

5.3.1 Two-Stage Serial Reduction

Two-stage serial reduction uses two valves in series to reduce or eliminate extreme variations between the inflow pressure and the final reduced outlet pressure. Two stage reduction is recommended when:

  • Initial pressures are 200 psi (14 bar) or greater, or
  • The desired pressure reduction ratio is greater than 4:1 (e.g., from 200 psi to 50 psi / 14 to 3.5 bar), or
  • The inflow pressure fluctuates greatly

The advantage is that neither valve is subjected to extreme pressure differentials, thus prolonging the life of the valves and delivering more precise pressure regulation.

5.3.2 Parallel Connection

Connecting two or more smaller size pressure reducing valves in parallel to serve a single supply main may be used where there is a wide variation in demand at the reduced pressure. Parallel installations offer:

  • Increased capacity where needed
  • Improved valve performance for widely variable demands
  • The ability to service individual valves without requiring a system to be shut down

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

減壓閥 (Pressure Reducing Valve, PRV): 將高壓供氣降低至製程所需工作壓力的閥件。選型原則：正常操作壓力應落在閥的能力範圍中段（mid-point），而非接近最大或最小值——這就像汽車引擎在最大轉速60%–80%時效率最好、壽命最長。

兩段串聯減壓 (Two-Stage Serial Reduction): 當入口壓力 ≥ 200 psi，或減壓比 > 4:1 時使用。邏輯是將大壓差分兩次承受，每個閥的壓差都在合理範圍內，精度更高、閥件壽命更長。

並聯連接 (Parallel Connection): 多個小PRV並聯，用於需求量變化大的供氣點。好處是可在不停機的狀態下輪流維護各個閥，這是GMP環境持續生產的重要設計考量。

重點提示：直接產品接觸氣體的材質要求

當氣體直接接觸藥品（如凍乾機頭空間充填氮氣），PRV的材質和表面處理（finish）就成為品質關鍵屬性（CQA）的一部分。此時需要考慮：316L不鏽鋼、電拋光（electropolished）內表面、無油脂裝配、以及材質相容性文件。ISPE指出這些對sterile operations是「critical」的——在法規意義上，這意味著需要有文件記錄的驗證依據。

減壓比判斷標準

判斷是否需要兩段串聯減壓：

條件1：入口壓力 ≥ 200 psi（14 bar）
條件2：減壓比 > 4:1
        例：200 psi → 50 psi = 4:1（邊界）
           200 psi → 40 psi = 5:1（需兩段）
條件3：入口壓力波動大

符合任一條件 → 建議採用兩段串聯減壓

兩段設計原則：
  第一段：從入口壓力降至中間壓力
  第二段：從中間壓力降至最終工作壓力
  每段壓差 ≤ 4:1 為佳

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的廠區鋼瓶供氣（通常2000 psi）降壓到製程使用壓力（例如100 psi），需要幾段減壓？為什麼？
  2. 並聯PRV設計為什麼特別適合CDMO環境？從連續生產的角度思考。
5.4 Mixing Valves — 混氣閥

原文內容 Original Text

A mixture of gases may be purchased pre-mixed and supplied through a dedicated system, or gases may be mixed at the POU using a mixing valve arrangement.

Gases may be mixed using a mass flow controller on each gas line. The mass flow controller is controlled by a flow sensor and feeds the gases into a static mixer.

Gas mixing systems can be accurate to ±1%.

Figure 5.2 shows an example configuration for a blending system. The blend ratio of the gases can be adjusted by varying the setpoint of the ratio setting of FY. The setpoints can be adjusted manually or automatically. If automatic blend composition control is needed, the blend composition should be measured and the composition controller should be arranged to act as the cascade master which is modulating the setpoint to FY.

"Gas mixing systems can be accurate to ±1%."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

混氣閥系統 (Gas Mixing / Blending System): 在製程現場即時混合兩種或以上氣體，常見應用：CO₂/N₂混合（用於生物反應器pH控制）、O₂/N₂混合（用於細胞培養）、N₂/CO₂（用於incubator環境控制）。

質量流量控制器 (Mass Flow Controller, MFC): 精確控制每種氣體質量流量的儀器，不受壓力和溫度變化影響（因為它測量的是質量，而非體積）。兩個MFC加上靜態混合器（static mixer）就構成基本的混氣系統。精度可達 ±1%。

預混 vs. 現場混合: 預混氣體（pre-mixed）方便，但每次換氣瓶的比例可能有批次差異；現場MFC混合精度高、可即時調整，適合比例需要頻繁變動的製程。

重點提示：混氣比例的驗證

在GMP環境中，混氣比例本身可能是一個關鍵製程參數（CPP）。例如，細胞培養基的CO₂濃度控制pH值，直接影響細胞生長和產品品質。因此，MFC的校驗記錄、靜態混合器的效能確認、以及混合後氣體的定期分析，都需要納入製程驗證計畫。±1%的精度聽起來很好，但需要有數據支持這個聲稱在你的特定條件下成立。

比喻說明 Analogy

MFC混氣系統就像高精度的調酒機——每種「材料」（氣體）都有精確的流量控制，混合比例可以程式設定並記錄。預混氣體瓶則像買現成的調酒包——方便，但每包的比例你要相信供應商的CoA。在需要嚴格控制的GMP製程中，你會選哪個？答案取決於你的CPP設計和風險評估。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. CO₂/N₂混氣用於生物反應器，混氣比例偏差±5%對產品品質有什麼影響？這個參數應該歸類為CPP嗎？
  2. 「級聯控制（cascade control）」在混氣系統中的意思是什麼？它解決了什麼問題？
5.5 Filtration — 過濾

原文內容 Original Text

5.5.1 Gas Filtration for Sterile Applications

Pharmaceutical gas distribution systems are usually protected with filters rated 1 µm or smaller at the generation source. Where sterile gas or sterile venting is required, this is usually provided by a 0.2 µm rated hydrophobic sterilizing grade filter at the points of delivery or use.

Sterile gas/vent filters can either be pre-sterilized by autoclaving and aseptically installed, or sterilized in situ by Steaming in Place (SIP). For single use bioreactors and other disposable systems, filters can be sterilized using gamma irradiation. Gas sterilizing filters usually incorporate 0.2 µm rated microporous membranes made of hydrophobic polytetrafluoroethylene (PTFE) or hydrophobic polyvinylidenefluoride (PVDF). Filters with PTFE membranes are not compatible with gamma irradiation.

Some 0.2 µm rated membrane filters are also rated for removal of airborne viruses down to 20 nm (0.020 µm) and airborne particles as fine as 0.003 µm. This is possible because filters are typically rated for particle/microbial size removal from liquids, whereas additional removal mechanisms occur in gases that enhance removal of particles finer than the liquid pore size rating.

Pharmaceutical grade gas sterilizing grade filters are normally provided with a CoA from the manufacturer. The manufacturer may perform non-destructive (integrity) testing on filters prior to shipment. Retention of bacteria under liquid challenge conditions is considered the most stringent qualification for critical gas sterilizing and venting applications.

Depending on user risk assessments and intended use, filters may be integrity tested:

  • prior to use
  • after use
  • at a predetermined interval
  • after events that are considered stress conditions for the filter (e.g., sterilization, high temperature air flow)

Critical use filters can be installed with POU integrity test ports that allow integrity testing in situ.

5.5.2 Filter Integrity Testing

Three methods for integrity testing of sterilizing gas filters are the:

  1. Bubble Point Pressure Test
  2. Forward Flow (Diffusion) Test
  3. Water Intrusion Test

5.5.2.1 Bubble Point Pressure Test

The Bubble Point Pressure test determines the installation integrity of a wetted filter by determining the gas pressure necessary to force the wetting liquid from the largest flow pathways or defects in the filter. For hydrophobic filters, the wetting liquid is usually a 70% IPA/30% water solution.

In a manual test, a length of tubing is connected to the downstream port of the filter assembly and the other end immersed in liquid. Bulk flow of gas is indicated by rapid bubbling. The pressure at which rapid bubbling is observed is recorded as the "Bubble Point Pressure." This procedure is not applicable to sterilized filters prior to their use, but may be utilized prior to sterilization or after use.

Automated instruments perform a Bubble Point Pressure test from the upstream side of the wetted filter — automated tests can be performed on sterilized filters before use. A pressure reading lower than the manufacturer's minimum recommended limit is an indication of integrity failure.

Bubble Point Pressure testing is less suited to high area cartridges and multi-cartridge assemblies due to the subjectivity of the endpoint detection.

5.5.2.2 Forward Flow (Diffusion) Test

The Forward Flow or "Diffusion" test determines the integrity of a wetted filter by quantitatively measuring gas flow at a gas test pressure set marginally below the minimum Bubble Point Pressure (typically at around 80%). The measured gas flow rate is empirically correlated to microbial retention.

Automated instruments perform a Forward Flow test from the upstream side of the filter — can be performed on sterilized filters before use without compromising downstream sterility. A Forward Flow rate higher than the manufacturer's maximum allowable specification is an indication of integrity test failure.

The Forward Flow or "Diffusion" test is a quantitative measurement suitable for high area cartridges and multi-cartridge assemblies. However, it is also limited by the requirement to wet the filter with a low surface tension liquid prior to testing and to dry it before returning it to service.

5.5.2.3 Water Intrusion Test

In the Water Intrusion Test, the integrity of a clean and dry hydrophobic membrane filter is determined by flooding the filter assembly with water, applying air overpressure to force water into the largest flow paths, or defects in the filter. Water flow through the filter is measured by pressure decay or by direct volumetric flow.

A flow rate higher than the manufacturer's maximum allowable limit is an indication of integrity test failure.

Water intrusion testing avoids the use of alcohol and does not contaminate the downstream of integral filters, making it particularly suitable for testing of sterile hydrophobic membrane filters in situ. However, it is limited by: the requirement to introduce and drain water from the upstream, higher false failure rates due to wet or contaminated filters, and sensitivity to temperature variation. It is not well suited for very small filter assemblies.

In operation, sterilizing gas filters are usually integrity tested before sterilization or after use by the Forward Flow (Diffusion) or Bubble Point Pressure tests. When testing filters in situ after sterilization, a variation of the Water Intrusion Test using an automated test instrument may be used.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：過濾的層次架構

製程氣體過濾系統是分層設計的——不是一個濾器解決所有問題，而是每個環節承擔不同的過濾任務：

  • 源頭保護（≤1 µm）：在氣體產生源（如壓縮機出口）安裝，去除大顆粒，保護下游設備
  • 使用點最終過濾（0.2 µm，無菌級）：產品接觸氣體的最後一道防線。這是「最後防線（last line of defense）」的意義——它是確保氣體無菌的主要屏障
  • PTFE vs. PVDF膜：兩者都是疏水性材質，但PTFE不相容伽馬滅菌，單次性系統（single-use）需選PVDF

重點提示：0.2 µm過濾器的「意外能力」

0.2 µm的液相額定孔徑，在氣相中可以去除小至0.003 µm的粒子，甚至病毒（20 nm = 0.020 µm）。原因在於：氣體中的顆粒去除機制（衝擊、攔截、擴散、靜電）比液體中更多元，過濾效率遠高於液相額定值的預期。這對製藥氣體設計是個重要的安全餘量知識。

三種完整性測試方法比較

方法              適用時機        優點              限制
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
泡點壓力測試      滅菌前/使用後   直觀、易理解      需潤濕；手動法不
(Bubble Point)                                      適用大濾芯；限滅
                                                    菌前使用（手動）

前向流測試        滅菌前/後均可   定量、可校驗；    需潤濕+乾燥復原；
(Forward Flow)   （自動化）      適合大濾芯        較費時

水侵入測試        原位滅菌後      無酒精；不污染    假失敗率較高；不
(Water Intrusion) 首選           下游；原位測試    適合小濾芯；溫度
                                                    敏感

比喻說明 Analogy

過濾器完整性測試就像出門前測試雨傘有沒有破洞。泡點測試是用嘴吹看有沒有漏氣（直觀但主觀）；前向流測試是用精密氣壓計量測洩漏量（客觀定量）；水侵入測試是把傘浸在水裡看有沒有水滲入（最適合現場原位測試，不用弄濕整支傘）。三種方法各有優缺點，GMP環境中根據時機和設備選擇最適合的。

實務應用 CDMO Validation Perspective

在無菌充填線，凍乾機和充填機的頭空間氮氣管路上的0.2 µm過濾器是「關鍵使用點過濾器」，需要：

  • 使用前完整性測試（或供應商CoA確認）
  • SIP後的Water Intrusion Test（原位，不破壞下游無菌性）
  • 使用後（或每批次後）的Forward Flow Test確認
  • 完整的更換記錄：日期、批號、測試結果、操作員簽名
  • 過濾器使用壽命驗證：SIP次數、使用時間、通氣量的上限

這些都是FDA查廠時必查的文件，缺少任一項都可能導致483 observation。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼PTFE膜濾器不能用伽馬射線滅菌？這對單次性生物反應器的設計意味著什麼？
  2. 水侵入測試（Water Intrusion Test）最大的優點是什麼？在什麼場景下你會優先選擇它？
  3. 過濾器完整性測試失敗，下一步的標準作業程序應該包括哪些步驟？
5.6 Filters in Compressed Air Systems — 壓縮空氣系統的過濾配置

原文內容 Original Text

The concepts described in this section can be applied to other process gas systems, depending on the risks associated with the gas supply source and the CQAs for a gas.

A suite of filters used in a commercial application may comprise the following filters:

5.6.1 Compressor or Source Gas Pre-Filter

Reduction of particulate on the gas feed can use lower cost filter media and installation methods than in-line filtration systems. This is therefore a cost effective filter and helps to prolong equipment life.

5.6.2 Compressor Discharge

It is considered good practice to install a moisture separator or coalescing filter and a general purpose filter on the discharge from the compressor. This should help to reduce the moisture and particulate build up in the receiver. Coalescing filters remove moisture droplets condensed by the compressor after cooler.

5.6.3 Pre-dryer Filtration

A general purpose filter will normally be used to remove particulate down to 1 µm and to help keep the drying media clean. The general purpose filter is usually used in conjunction with a high efficiency oil/hydrocarbon removal filter, to remove any atmospheric contamination and particulate down to 0.01 µm.

5.6.4 Post Dryer Filtration

After the dryer, a similar suite of filters will be used to prevent any particulate migration from the dryer into the system. For oil-lubricated compressors, the high efficiency oil/hydrocarbon coalescing filter is used here as a means of particulate control (oil-less compressors do not require coalescing filters).

After a gas storage system (receiver), filter sets are usually provided as parallel systems. This allows for replacement of a filter while the system is kept operational.

5.6.5 Post Receiver Filters

A final filter is normally used before the distribution system to ensure that the gas entering the distribution system meets required specifications. For sterile applications this may be a 0.2 µm rated membrane filter, which will need to be sterilized. For oral solid dose applications, a 0.45 µm or 1 µm rated filter may be suitable.

5.6.6 Alternative Post Dryer Filter Arrangement

For small systems, where there is a very low risk that system operation and maintenance could affect gas quality, POU filtration may be considered unnecessary. A robust post dryer filter arrangement may be considered as an alternative:

  • The post dryer filter set may be arranged as a "double" set of gas filters, with a second set in series acting as a "policing" filter set. The gas quality is checked in normal operation on the pre-filter set; if a gas fails a test, the second set of filters should ensure that the gas will be re-filtered prior to entering the system. During system maintenance the final set of filters are used to replace the pre-filter set and new filters are installed in the final location, minimizing operating cost.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：壓縮空氣過濾的五層架構

ISPE描述的是一個完整的「過濾縱深防禦」系統，每一層都有特定的目的：

  • 入口預過濾：低成本去除大顆粒，保護壓縮機本體
  • 壓縮機出口：去除壓縮冷凝後的水滴（聚結過濾器）+ 一般性顆粒
  • 乾燥前過濾：保護乾燥劑不被油污和顆粒污染（0.01 µm油氣去除）
  • 乾燥後過濾：防止乾燥劑顆粒遷移進入配送系統
  • 儲槽後/進入配送前：最終的粒徑把關（0.2 µm for sterile）

比喻說明 Analogy

壓縮空氣的多層過濾就像城市的自來水淨化：水庫（粗濾/沉澱）→ 快濾池（去除懸浮物）→ 活性碳（去除有機物/味道）→ 加氯消毒→ 家用濾水器（最終使用點）。每一步都有特定的污染物目標，沒有哪一步是多餘的。在藥廠，0.2 µm的POU過濾器就是那個「家用濾水器」——它保護的是直接接觸藥品的最後一段路。

重點提示：並聯過濾器組的GMP意義

儲槽後的過濾器「並聯設計」是一個重要的GMP操作彈性：一組在線運作，另一組可以在不停機的情況下更換。這解決了一個常見的CDMO痛點——更換過濾器通常需要排程停機，影響批次生產計畫。並聯設計讓過濾器更換變成一個「不需要停批的例行維護」。在過濾器更換記錄中，這種「在線更換」的設計也需要有對應的SOP和更換確認程序。

實務應用：「哨兵過濾器」設計在CDMO的價值

5.6.6的「雙重串聯（policing filter）」概念特別適合中小型CDMO或實驗室生產線：

  • 主過濾器失效時，哨兵過濾器自動接手，產品不受影響
  • 維護時輪換：舊的哨兵成為主濾，裝新過濾器成為新哨兵——Zero downtime
  • 節省POU安裝過濾器的成本（某些情況下可以取消POU個別過濾）

前提是風險評估確認系統夠乾淨，且文件記錄完整。這個設計在查廠時需要能解釋清楚邏輯。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 無油壓縮機（oil-free compressor）相比油潤滑壓縮機，在過濾需求上有什麼差異？在GMP成本分析中如何評估？
  2. 「哨兵過濾器」設計適合取代POU濾器的條件是什麼？什麼情況下無論如何都不能省略POU過濾？
5.7 Material Selection — 材質選擇

原文內容 Original Text

Factors which should be considered when selecting materials of construction for a distribution system include:

  • potential impact on the desired gas quality attributes
  • local regulations
  • robustness
  • installation time
  • local custom and practice
  • insurer's requirements
  • cost

Materials used for a process gas distribution system and associated equipment should be resistant to adverse effects of the gas being transported. They should also comply with the necessary national and local regulations for a gas.

The effects of the environment on the external surfaces of the distribution system (e.g., cleaning and maintenance) should be considered. For example, copper may not be resistant to cleaning materials and may develop a surface coating (by oxidation) which may shed particles, so copper is usually not used within a production area; however, copper may be acceptable outside a production area.

5.7.1 Moisture Ingress

Materials used for distribution systems should provide a robust vapor barrier to prevent an increase in the moisture levels of a gas. Vapor ingress can be a significant issue for flexible POU pipes. Careful selection of fittings is also necessary where moisture ingress may affect critical attributes, e.g., pneumatic push-in fittings can lead to moisture ingress.

5.7.2 Particulate Generation

Once any loose material in a process gas distribution system has been blown out, particulate generation is not usually an issue in relation to a gas, even for carbon steel. Steel does not normally corrode if the Relative Humidity (RH) is below 35%. At the low Pressure Dewpoints (PDPs) typically used in pharmaceutical systems, carbon or galvanized steel would not normally be a source of particulate.

Where the installation is exposed in a classified area, the risk of particulate shedding from the external surface of the pipe work should be considered.

5.7.3 Ease of Assembly and Modification

Ease of assembly together with cost/installation time/robustness in use have a major impact and may give different results depending on the application. Copper pipe may be the material of choice for a distribution system, whereas stainless tube with compression fittings may be used locally for a specific piece of equipment.

5.7.4 Availability of Fittings

"Push fit" fittings are not usually specified as sanitary, so require careful consideration before use. Suppliers should have a readily accessible source of fittings to ensure that a system can be maintained over its entire lifetime. The use of "special" fittings during construction may become costly to maintain.

5.7.5 Pipe Work Support Requirements

Some materials used for pipe work can require a higher number of supports, which can increase installation costs. Additional supports also may be required where a system is subject to rapid changes in pressure or extremes of temperature. Where ball valves are used, these can induce movement in pipe work and additional supports may be required.

5.7.6 Optional Materials

Material selection is dependent on the risks the interaction between the gas and materials of construction presents to the end user. Decision processes should be documented and checked.

5.7.6.1 Stainless Steel

Stainless steel is usually used in production areas:

  • ASTM 304 grade stainless steel may be adequate for non-sterile manufacturing areas, but there may be a risk of corrosion depending on the cleaning and sanitizing materials used.
  • For sterile operations, ASTM 316 grade or equivalent is normally used, as the cleaning and sanitizing materials used are generally more corrosive.

Sanitary jointing methods are not usually required, as there is slight risk of microbial growth within a dry system. Orbital welding may be specified to ensure consistent reliable welds, with a purge gas used to prevent oxide formation inside pipe work.

It may be cost effective to specify lower grade stainless steel (e.g., ASTM 304) for distribution systems, with a higher grade used in production areas where it will be subject to more corrosive cleaning agents.

5.7.6.2 Medical Grade Copper

Medical gas grade copper (e.g., ASTM B 280, ISO 7396-1, BS EN13348) may be used in major installations (100 ft / 30.5 m of pipe or more). Material should be specified as clean and degreased, purged during fabrication, and jointed without flux using "hard" or silver solder.

Copper pipe may be used for a distribution system, with a break at a service outlet panel or service void, with the final part of the pipe work in stainless steel within a production area. Copper pipe may not be recommended for use with nitrogen, as moisture in the gas may cause internal corrosion.

5.7.6.3 Plastics

Modern thermoplastic (e.g., high density polyethylene, HDPE) can be used for the clean distribution of gases. Thick walled HDPE pipe is available, suited to compressed gases up to 160 psi (11 bar). Disadvantages of plastic pipe work include:

  • Systems may require additional supports
  • Additional expansion requirements over metal systems
  • Ultra violet stability for external applications should be checked
  • Plastic material cannot be used for a flammable or oxidizing gas
  • The plastic may not present such a high quality vapor barrier as metals

In some regions, OSHA regulates against using brittle plastics for compressed air distribution systems.

5.7.6.4 Aluminum

Proprietary systems using aluminum pipe work may be limited in size and connected using plastic push-in connectors. These systems should not be used for a flammable or oxidizing gas.

5.7.6.5 Carbon Steel

Where a gas is kept at a low Relative Humidity (RH) (below 35%), risk of internal corrosion is minimal; therefore, steel is an option for use in a distribution system. If used, galvanized material is usually selected to provide a corrosion resistant external finish.

Jointing has to be specified carefully, to ensure minimal risk of generating loose material or contaminating inside a pipe with hydrocarbon, e.g., welding with a purge gas, or screwed joints made without lubricant/sealant, using non-shedding material such as PTFE tape. For these reasons as well as the general appearance, carbon steel is not generally used.

Testing and Cleaning

Materials specified for use in a processed gas system should be specified to be free of particulates and any hydrocarbon. They should be shipped and stored on site wrapped and sealed. Before use on site, system fittings and components should be inspected to ensure that the internal finishes are as specified and not marked or damaged. A GMP protocol should be used to ensure the system is kept clean during construction, e.g.:

  • no opening left open
  • only clean tools used
  • tools marked for their purpose

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：材質選擇的七個考量維度

ISPE列出的七個因素（品質影響、法規、耐用性、安裝時間、在地習慣、保險要求、成本）不是等重的。在GMP環境中，決策優先順序必須遵循：

品質影響（對氣體CQA的影響）
▼
法規與安全合規
▼
耐用性、安裝便利性、成本

材質選擇的文件記錄（decision documentation）必須反映這個優先順序，否則在查廠時很難解釋為什麼選了某種材料。

重點提示：銅管在GxP環境的使用限制

銅管是醫療氣體系統的傳統材料，但在藥廠GMP環境中有兩個重要限制：

  1. 產品區域不適用：銅在含氯或強鹼清潔劑環境中會氧化，氧化物可能脫落成顆粒污染——生產區域清潔頻率高、清潔劑更強，故銅管通常止步於服務廊道，不進入生產區。
  2. 氮氣系統慎用：若氮氣品質不夠乾燥（含水份），銅管內表面會腐蝕。ISPE特別提出這個警告——尤其對於低露點要求的高純氮氣系統，銅管是不適合的材料。

不鏽鋼等級選擇指南

區域              建議等級      原因
─────────────────────────────────────────────
非無菌生產區       ASTM 304     一般腐蝕性低
無菌生產區         ASTM 316L    耐氯化物、耐強鹼
                              （含Mo，抗點蝕性更強）
直接產品接觸氣體   316L + 電拋光  表面粗糙度Ra ≤ 0.5 µm
                  (electropolished)  降低微粒附著、易於清潔

電拋光（Electropolishing）：
  用電化學法去除表面微凸起，
  使表面光滑均勻（"passive layer"更完整）
  → 微粒產生風險最低
  → 產品接觸氣體的黃金標準

軌道焊接（Orbital Welding）：
  自動化焊接，確保焊縫品質一致
  配合惰性保護氣（purge gas）防止內表面氧化
  → 無菌系統管路焊接的標準做法

比喻說明 Analogy

材質選擇就像裝修廚房選水槽——一般家用可以選不鏽鋼普通款；如果你開的是米其林餐廳，你可能要選衛生級（sanitary grade）拋光不鏽鋼，縫隙設計要能完全清潔到位。銅管就像漂亮的銅製水龍頭——外觀好看，但在強力洗碗機的環境中（高頻強力清洗）不是最佳選擇。材質選擇的最終測試是：這個材料在你廠的清潔和使用條件下，能在整個系統壽命周期內保持品質一致嗎？

實務應用：FDA查廠氣體系統材質檢查清單

查察官在審查氣體配送系統材質時通常會查：

  • 材質選擇依據文件：為什麼選這種材料？是否有書面的決策理由？
  • 材質證明書（Material Certificate）：符合ASTM 316L/304等規格的測試報告
  • 電拋光/表面處理記錄：直接產品接觸管路的表面粗糙度測試結果
  • 焊接記錄：軌道焊接的焊工資格、保護氣紀錄、焊縫檢驗記錄（視覺/內視鏡）
  • 系統驗收測試（SAT）：竣工後的吹掃記錄、微粒測試、露點確認
  • P&ID：配送系統的管路儀表圖是否與現場一致（As-built document）

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 同一棟廠房，走廊段用銅管、進入無菌生產區改用316L不鏽鋼——這種混合設計在哪個節點需要特別的品質控制措施？
  2. HDPE管路用於惰性氣體配送（如氮氣），它的蒸汽屏障（vapor barrier）性能不如金屬管。在什麼條件下這個缺點會變成實際問題？
  3. 建設期間的「清潔施工協議（GMP protocol during construction）」的目的是什麼？如果施工期間發生污染，如何確保最終系統品質？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • 配送架構：Ring main（環形主管）是GMP藥廠的首選——雙向供氣自平衡、可分段維護、支援多壓縮機冗餘，特別適合有未來擴廠計畫的CDMO。
  • 非回流閥：是防止逆流污染的實體屏障，必須盡量靠近POU安裝，高風險製程需要冗餘設計和定期功能測試（測試口設計是關鍵）。
  • 減壓閥：入口壓力 ≥ 200 psi 或減壓比 > 4:1 時必須採用兩段串聯設計；並聯PRV可在不停機狀態下輪換維護。
  • 過濾系統：「最後防線」是POU的 0.2 µm 疏水性滅菌級濾器（PTFE或PVDF膜）；三種完整性測試（泡點、前向流、水侵入）各有適用時機，Water Intrusion Test最適合原位滅菌後測試。
  • 壓縮空氣過濾層次：從源頭預過濾 → 出口聚結過濾 → 乾燥前除油 → 乾燥後去粒子 → 進入配送前最終過濾，層層設防、並聯設計支援不停機更換。
  • 材質選擇：無菌生產區選316L不鏽鋼（需電拋光+軌道焊接），直接產品接觸管路更需文件化決策依據；銅管不進生產區、不用於氮氣系統；塑膠管不用於可燃/氧化性氣體。
  • 查廠準備：材質證明書、焊接記錄、完整性測試記錄、P&ID As-built文件、過濾器更換日誌——這六類文件在FDA查廠時必須隨時能取出。
4

Chapter 4: Control & Monitoring Systems (Ch 6)

管控與監測系統 | p69-p80

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases | p69–p80

本章學習目標

  • 理解製程氣體管控系統的三大類別：壓縮空氣系統、鋼瓶系統、現場產氣與槽儲系統，及各自的控制邏輯
  • 掌握品質監測的核心參數：壓力、露點（水分）、微生物、微粒、碳氫化合物，並了解每項參數為何對藥廠製程至關重要
  • 了解取樣策略設計原則：POU取樣位置、過濾器前後的選擇依據，以及樣品代表性的確認方法
  • 熟悉各種水分監測技術（冷鏡、電解、阻抗、高分子薄膜）的原理與適用場合
  • 連結CDMO實務：製程氣體OOS事件如何觸發批次偏差調查，並影響放行決策
6.1 Introduction — 導論

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Control and monitoring systems may act as a risk mitigation tool in process gas systems.

Where appropriate in this chapter, a distinction is made between process gas systems and compressed air systems based upon differences in ownership and responsibility; compressed air systems are usually owned by an organization, whereas process gas storage/generation systems are usually rented from a specialist supplier.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

管控與監測系統 (Control and Monitoring Systems): 這章的核心主張是：監測系統本身就是風險緩解工具。換言之，即便氣體品質偶爾波動，只要能即時偵測並觸發響應（自動關閥、發出警報、啟動備用設備），就能防止不合規氣體流入製程。

所有權差異的重要性： 壓縮空氣系統由工廠自有，儀器校正、維護、文件都在廠內GMP體系下管理。製程氣體（N₂、CO₂、Ar）通常租自氣體供應商——他們有自己的控制系統，但廠方仍須確保這些系統的告警信號能接入廠內監控。

比喻說明 Analogy

這個所有權區分就像大樓的電力系統（工廠自有、自管）vs 外租的備用發電機（廠商維護，但你需要知道它的電量與故障信號）。兩者都要能接入你的中央控制室，才能完整掌握廠務安全。

重點提示 Key Notes

當製程氣體由外部供應商提供時，廠方可能需要複製安裝監測儀表（duplicate monitoring instruments），目的是：(1) 讓氣體供應商用他自己的標準儀器；(2) 廠方用自己管理校正的儀器，確保數據符合GMP文件要求。兩套儀器並行，不互相依賴。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果氣體供應商的控制系統發出警報，但廠方BMS沒有接收到信號，可能的後果是什麼？
  2. 為什麼廠方要自行管理監測儀表的校正，而不完全依賴氣體供應商的數據？
6.2 Control Systems — 管控系統

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

There are three categories of system which are controlled:

  • Compressed Air Systems
  • Cylinder Systems
  • On Site Gas Generation and Bulk Storage Systems

6.2.1 Compressed Air Systems

The compressors normally have a specific proprietary control system. This should control and monitor the compressor, shutting it down in the event of an alarm or sensor failure in order to protect the equipment. Usually compressor control is based on maintaining a minimum pressure at its discharge – on a basic system through shutting down or starting up the compressor, on a more sophisticated system through regulating the compressor output.

There is usually provision for interconnecting these control systems or linking them through a "supervisory" controller that will manage multiple compressors, usually rotating the primary duty unit to ensure equal use of each system.

The dryers within a system typically come with a supplier's proprietary control system. The control systems typically operate based on a timer to control the sequence of operation between the two dryer vessels or the changeover between vessels is controlled by the discharge pressure dewpoint. The latter system is considered more energy efficient.

In the event of a system failure, the alarm from a dryer pressure dewpoint monitor may be used to automatically close the valve downstream of the dryer, as this would prevent putting potentially wet air into a distribution system – where a sudden loss of supply would create problems, this signal could also initiate a standby dryer.

The system status and any system alarms can be fed through a Building Management System (BMS) to facilitate remote monitoring, and management of any alarms.

6.2.1.1 Cylinder Systems

There are two basic types of cylinder systems:

  1. Manual Changeover
  2. Automatic Changeover

Manual Changeover: These require the standby cylinder to be manually selected when the duty cylinder runs on low pressure. These basic systems do not provide capability for remote monitoring, though a low cylinder pressure switch may be provided for connection to either a local alarm, an alarm in the area in which the gas is used, or to a BMS.

Automatic Changeover: The system automatically changes over from a duty to a standby cylinder, and will give an alarm signal to notify the system owner that the empty cylinder needs to be changed. This may be connected to a local alarm, an alarm in the area in which the gas is used, or to a BMS.

6.2.2 On Site Generation Systems and Bulk Storage Systems

These systems are typically supplied and maintained by a specialist supplier; with their own control and monitoring systems.

The design and operation of these systems should be understood by the user, and alarm signals from the system made available for connection to a monitoring system, as required. Users may duplicate monitoring instruments for connection to their monitoring system to allow the gas system supplier to provide a standard package. This also has the advantage that the user retains management of the calibration of the devices.

The integration and monitoring of process gas systems should be considered during the design phase to ensure that the optimum solution is specified.

Where there are defined Lower Explosive Limits (LELs) for gas concentrations, monitoring systems and local safety alarms may be required by local regulations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

三類系統的管控邏輯差異：

  • 壓縮空氣系統： 廠方完整擁有，從壓縮機到乾燥機到配管都需納入GMP體系。控制邏輯以「維持最低出口壓力」為核心。
  • 鋼瓶系統： 最簡單——人工切換或自動切換。管理重點是確保備用鋼瓶在位、壓力低點告警能傳遞到值班人員或BMS。
  • 現場產氣/大型槽儲： 複雜度最高，通常由氣體公司遠程監控，廠方需整合其告警信號到自己的BMS或DCS。

露點控制換向 vs 計時換向

乾燥機雙塔切換有兩種邏輯：

  • 計時換向（Timer-based）： 固定時間切換，簡單但不考慮實際乾燥效果，可能提前切換（浪費能源）或延遲切換（露點惡化）。
  • 露點換向（Dewpoint-controlled）： 偵測出口露點，只在實際需要時才切換，更節能、更穩定。ISPE明確指出此方式更佳。

關鍵安全邏輯：若露點監測器發出警報，應自動關閉下游閥門，防止潮濕空氣進入配管。

比喻說明 Analogy

手動換鋼瓶就像手動加油站——你要自己去確認油量低了再換。自動切換系統則像現代汽車油箱：油位低自動亮燈，且在舊桶用完前就已切換到備用桶，不間斷供應。對於藥廠的連續製程，自動切換是基本要求，否則氣體中斷可能直接造成批次失敗。

重點提示 Key Notes — LEL 爆炸下限

Lower Explosive Limit (LEL，爆炸下限)： 可燃性氣體（如氫氣）在空氣中達到某濃度時才會爆炸，LEL是最低引爆濃度。例如氫氣LEL約4%（v/v）。

N₂和CO₂本身不可燃，但高濃度會造成缺氧窒息危害，需要氧氣不足警報（O₂ deficiency alarm）而非LEL警報。這是CDMO安全管理上的常見誤解——必須根據氣體特性選擇正確的安全監測類型。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在CDMO的無菌充填廠，N₂覆蓋（nitrogen blanketing）用於防止配方氧化。若N₂鋼瓶採用手動切換且未及時更換，導致N₂供應中斷，充填腔體可能進入空氣，造成O₂濃度上升、產品氧化降解——這是一個直接影響批次品質的OOS事件，需要完整偏差調查。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在設計階段未考慮BMS整合，日後要補接氣體系統告警信號，會面臨哪些驗證文件上的挑戰？
  2. 露點換向乾燥機（dewpoint-controlled）和計時換向乾燥機在GMP文件記錄上有何差異？哪種更容易舉證合規？
6.3.1 Operational Parameter Monitoring — 操作參數監測

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Pressure is often categorized as a CPP (Critical Process Parameter) for a process gas system, usually introducing a concomitant calibration and monitoring regime.

The gas supply system may be controlled by the pressure, either in the system receiver or in the entry point to the distribution system.

The distribution system should be sized so that end users receive the necessary flow and associated inlet pressure, based on design usage diversity or calculated pressure drop under peak usage.

"This Guide proposes that the pressure is usually an engineering parameter and not a CPP."

The basis for this is:

  • Any piece of equipment supplied by the gas system that has a requirement for a specific flow/pressure will have an inlet pressure switch that monitors and alarms for that use; this is a critical location/instrument.
  • The system pressure control provides a general indication, but does not monitor at each POU, or consider any usage, or effect at an individual POU.

It may be appropriate to review specific installations to determine if that rationale is appropriate.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

壓力：是CPP還是工程參數？ 這是ISPE提出的一個重要觀點。傳統上許多廠房把供氣幹管壓力列為CPP，配上嚴格的校正計畫。但ISPE認為，幹管壓力只是「大方向」指標，真正重要的是每個使用點（POU, Point of Use）的入口壓力。

邏輯推論： 幹管壓力正常，不代表最遠端POU的壓力足夠（因為有壓降）。因此，真正的關鍵是在設備入口安裝壓力開關，直接監測設備可用的氣體壓力。

公式與計算 Formula

壓力分配設計邏輯：

幹管設計壓力 = 最遠端POU需求壓力
             + 管路壓降（由流量、管徑計算）
             + 安全裕度

Peak usage 壓降需以最大同時使用量計算
（diversity factor 多樣性係數）

比喻說明 Analogy

幹管壓力就像城市自來水主幹管的水壓——市政局知道主幹壓力正常，但你家頂層浴室的水壓夠不夠，要看你家的供水設計。製程氣體也一樣：關鍵在於每個設備「入口」的壓力，而非系統層面的幹管壓力。

重點提示 Key Notes

ISPE這個建議具有實質的成本含義：把幹管壓力降級為「工程參數」，可以減少校正負擔（calibration burden）和文件要求。但這需要在URS（用戶需求規格）中明確說明，並在DQ/IQ/OQ文件中留下完整的風險評估理由。若監管機構在查廠時提問，廠方需能清楚說明為何不將幹管壓力視為CPP。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 如果你的無菌充填機需要最低5 bar N₂入口壓力，你會在哪個位置安裝壓力開關？警報下限設在幾bar比較合理？
  2. 在peak usage期間（多台設備同時用氣），如何確認幹管壓力不會因壓降過大而影響最遠端設備？
6.3.2 Quality Monitoring — 品質監測

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Quality monitoring is required at POUs located in controlled room environments. Regulations require that the particulate and microbiological quality of the compressed gas be equal to or better than that of the air in the environment into which the gas is introduced (at rest). (See Eudralex Volume 4 Annex-1, 2004; 21 CFR Part 210.)

Process gas systems may be operated at very low dewpoints or negative dewpoints, in accordance with user requirements. A properly operated process gas system with low moisture should not support the growth or survival of microorganisms.

The quantity of water necessary to support microbiological growth is usually expressed as water activity (aw). For gases, water activity is related to relative humidity (RH = aw × 100%) and also dewpoint which may be used to express moisture in a compressed gas. Molds and yeasts do not grow where the aw is less than 0.6 and bacteria do not grow where the aw is less than 0.85 (Scott et al., 2001).

Process gas systems are not normally designed to be sterilized. Control of microorganisms is usually accomplished at the POUs by using 0.2 μm sterilizing grade filters.

Low moisture environments may be used to preserve pharmaceutical products but may not prevent survival of microorganisms:

  1. Desiccation has been a long recognized method for short term preservation of microbiological cultures. Desiccated microorganisms have a variable death rate and a sizable population would have to be introduced into a system to be detectable downstream.
  2. Bacteria may also survive through the production of endospores. Endospores are tough, dormant non-reproductive structures produced by bacteria with the primary function to ensure survival through periods of environmental stress. Endospores may persist indefinitely in a dormant state awaiting conditions favorable for sporulation or return to vegetative growth.

Where the user requirements are particularly demanding, the requirement to ensure that a process gas system facilitates cleaning activities may be included, and the design specified accordingly (e.g., facilitate complete drainage).

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

品質等同原則（Quality Equivalence Principle）： 製程氣體進入潔淨室時，其微粒與微生物品質必須等於或優於所在潔淨室的靜態等級。例如在ISO 5 / EU Grade A環境下操作，送入的N₂品質也必須達到ISO 5等級。這是Annex 1和21 CFR Part 210的明確要求。

Water Activity (水活性, aw): 表示系統中可供微生物利用的「自由水」量。aw = 1 為純水，aw < 0.6 幾乎沒有生物能存活。乾燥氣體（低露點）的aw接近0，理論上不利於微生物生長——但這不等於無菌！

重點提示 Key Notes — 內孢子的威脅

Endospores (內孢子/芽孢)： 這是理解乾燥氣體微生物風險的關鍵。芽孢桿菌（Bacillus）等細菌在惡劣環境下形成芽孢，可在極端乾燥、高溫、輻射條件下存活數十年。

換言之：乾燥氣體可以抑制微生物生長，但無法殺滅芽孢。一旦氣體到達有水分、有營養的環境（如產品），芽孢可能復活。這就是為何產品接觸型氣體必須使用0.2 µm滅菌級過濾器，而不能僅靠低露點來保證微生物安全。

比喻說明 Analogy

芽孢就像植物的種子：在沙漠裡（乾燥氣體中）靜止不動，一旦遇水（產品中的水分）就會發芽生長。乾燥的管路好比沙漠，種子在裡面不生長，但並未消失。0.2 µm過濾器才是真正的「擋種子」屏障。

微生物生長界限 Water Activity Thresholds

aw < 0.60  →  黴菌、酵母菌無法生長（Molds & Yeasts）
aw < 0.85  →  一般細菌無法生長（Most Bacteria）
aw < 0.91  →  大部分致病菌無法生長

關係換算：
RH (%) = aw × 100
aw = 0.6 約等於 RH 60%
極低露點（如 -40°C dp）→ RH <1% → aw << 0.01

實務應用 CDMO Application

在無菌充填線（aseptic filling line）的N₂覆蓋設計中：最終使用點（POU）應安裝0.2 µm滅菌過濾器，並定期進行完整性測試（integrity test）。微生物監測取樣點應設在過濾器上游（pre-filter），因為過濾器後取樣可能因取樣行為本身引入污染風險（暴露了已滅菌的流路）。這與ISPE 6.3.2的取樣策略討論直接對應。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的廠使用N₂進行無菌充填的氣體覆蓋，且依賴低露點（-60°C）控制微生物風險。FDA查廠官員問你「你如何確保芽孢不會污染產品？」你如何回答？
  2. 非無菌口服液製程中的CO₂充填用氣，需要監測微生物嗎？如果需要，監測哪類微生物？
6.3.2.1 Test Method Considerations — 測試方法考量

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Test method(s) normally depend on the types of microorganisms that are desired to be detected. Factors that should be considered include the:

  • drug product(s) manufactured within the facility
  • type of process gas
  • regulatory controls
  • manufacturing processes

The drug product manufacturing associated risks should be considered. Parenteral drug products are manufactured to be sterile; therefore, the process gas should be rendered sterile prior to use in the manufacturing process. Non-sterile drug products may be manufactured using process gases that are not rendered sterile; therefore, the introduction of objectionable microorganisms should be considered.

A risk assessment should be used to develop a rationale for the sample point strategy.

Process gas systems may be designed and controlled using combinations of inline and POU filters. Monitoring strategies for inline and POU filter sample locations should be considered. Monitoring may occur upstream or downstream of a filter, or duplex filters may be required.

For example, in the case of gas supply to a sterile operation (e.g., nitrogen blanketing during aseptic filling processes), the process gas sample should be taken before the final sterile filter. As this gas is 0.2 µm filtered for particulate, the process gas quality should be the same pre- and post- the sterile final filter.

To take a clean compressed air sample after the sterile filter requires the sampling site to follow the same level of sterilization as the unit operation. Sampling after a final filter poses a potential risk to the unit operation each time a sample is taken.

Design of sample points should avoid piping common to other utilities such as high purity waters and pure steam.

A sample should represent the quality at a POU; the location used should be demonstrated to represent the quality at the POU.

The type of process gas should be considered. Process air and O₂ should be monitored for aerobic microorganisms. Reduced oxygen content gases such as N₂, CO₂, and Ar should be monitored for microorganisms capable of anaerobic growth.

The size of a sample can affect the monitoring method chosen. Sample size may be based on the sample size required for room classification (in accordance with ISO-14644). A sample size of 0.7 m³ would be required for ISO 5 environments.

Process gas distribution systems are not environmentally classified.

A gas generation and distribution process is a closed environment, with minimal risk of contamination from an external source. Contaminants in pipe work are most likely to come from the process gas or the pipe work; therefore, a sample taken from the longest pipe run is the most likely to find issues resulting from this cause of contamination.

Inclusion of 0.2 μm sterilizing grade filters at a POU can ensure that process gas quality at a POU is equal to or better than that of the air in the environment into which the gas is introduced.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

取樣位置策略（Sampling Location Strategy）： ISPE的關鍵建議是將取樣點設在最終滅菌過濾器「上游」（before the final sterile filter）。原因有二：

  • 過濾器上游的氣體品質 = 過濾器下游的品質（因為0.2 µm過濾器截留所有微粒和微生物）
  • 在過濾器下游取樣，每次取樣都會打開已滅菌流路，引入外部污染風險——這是重複性的製程風險，不可接受。

最長管路（Longest Pipe Run）： 封閉管路系統的污染主要來自管路內部（管材、焊接點、滯留液體），因此最長管路的終端最可能累積問題，是最具挑戰性的取樣點。

好氧 vs 厭氧微生物監測

這是容易忽視的細節：

  • 壓縮空氣、O₂供應： 環境含氧，監測好氧菌（aerobic microorganisms）
  • N₂、CO₂、Ar供應： 低氧環境，監測厭氧菌（anaerobic microorganisms）
  • ISPE特別指出：性能測試期間若確認無好氧菌，常規監測可只看厭氧菌（低氧氣體系統）。這是科學化的降負荷設計，但需要文件支持。

重點提示 Key Notes — 取樣體積

ISO 14644-1規定ISO 5環境的微粒取樣體積為0.7 m³。製程氣體品質需達到ISO 5等級的系統，應以相同體積取樣，確保統計可信度。

注意：ISO 8573-7（壓縮空氣微生物標準）建議用1 m³，但業界實際採用並不廣泛。對於日常監測，較小體積（如1立方英尺）也被接受，但初始驗證測試應使用較大體積。

比喻說明 Analogy

在最終過濾器後取樣就像：醫護人員剛完成手術器械滅菌，然後打開包裝來「檢驗」是否無菌——每次開包就是一次污染機會。正確做法是在滅菌前確認品質，以及定期對過濾器本身做完整性測試，而非在使用中反覆取樣。

實務應用 CDMO Application — OOS事件處理

假設你的N₂微生物監測在最長管路取樣點偵測到厭氧菌超出行動限（Action Limit），CDMO的標準響應流程：

  1. 立即隔離： 停止使用該管路氣體，評估批次衝擊
  2. 根本原因調查： 檢查過濾器完整性、管路死角、最近維護記錄
  3. 批次衝擊評估： 問「是否有產品接觸到此氣體？」、「過濾器是否在位且完好？」
  4. 整改： 管路消毒/清洗、過濾器更換，並重新取樣確認
  5. 文件： 完整偏差報告、CAPA，必要時報告給客戶和監管機構

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你廠有三條N₂使用點管路，長度分別為10m、50m、120m。常規微生物監測應重點監測哪條管路？為什麼？
  2. 製程氣體配管系統「未進行環境等級分類」這句話的實際意涵是什麼？代表可以放寬監測要求嗎？
6.3.2.2 Microbial Monitoring — 微生物監測方法

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Methods existing for monitoring environments may be extended to monitor process gases. The recovery medium for the microorganisms should include the growth media used in the environmental monitoring program for room air, surfaces, and personnel (PDA Technical Report No. 13), as a minimum. The medium should include the demonstrated ability to support the growth of a variety of bacteria and fungi.

The sample device should be sanitizable or sterilizable prior to collection of each microbiological sample. Validation or performance qualification of the method should be considered prior to implementation.

Impaction Methods

Slit to Agar Sampler: This method uses a revolving agar plate located at a specified distance from a slit orifice to impinge the sample air flow onto an agar surface. This device can sample a large volume of gas and can provide a time versus concentration relationship. The equipment is large, requires 150 mm agar plates, and is difficult to sanitize.

Impact Sampler: Pulls a stream of air through a metal plate containing many small and evenly spaced holes onto an agar surface. These samplers for process gases are relatively large and difficult to sanitize; however, the entire sample flow path and impaction plate can be steam sterilized. These units have the advantage of sampling a cubic meter of gas in less than ten minutes.

Centrifugal Sampler: These samplers use a fan to pull a cylinder shaped cone of air into the sample head and particles or microorganisms are deposited by centrifugal force onto an agar strip. The sample head can be steam sterilized and the units are light in weight. Special agar strips are required. Special adapters for sampling process gases are available.

Filtration

Filtration is a simple to use and low cost method for monitoring microorganisms in process gases, relative to methods requiring instrumentation. When numerous sample points should be monitored on a regular basis, it may be less costly to stock multiple filter holders than multiple sample instruments.

The method consists of a type of filter holder (plastic or stainless steel), sterile filters, and a calibrated flow meter. The appropriate volume of gas is filtered through the filter and the filter is aseptically transferred to an agar medium for growth and enumeration. The membrane usually has a nominal pore size rating of 0.45 μm.

Membrane Filter Materials

Membrane filters for environmental monitoring may be made of:

  • cellulose nitrate
  • cellulose acetate
  • mixed cellulose esters
  • Polyethersulfone (PES)
  • hydrophilic PVDF
  • gelatin
  • nylon

Users should verify that the filter does not inhibit the recovery of indicator microorganisms. A cubic meter sample may be collected in a twelve minute time period. Gelatin membrane filters are not suitable for compressed gas monitoring.

Liquid Impingement

Liquid impingement methods use a liquid to trap and collect microorganisms. The stream of gas is directed through an orifice at high velocity into the liquid. Microorganisms are forced into the liquid and removed from the gas stream.

Disadvantages may include a glass construction resulting in a fragile device. Improper sample handling may result in false positive data. The method should be qualified to demonstrate that it does not destroy vegetative microorganisms.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts — 四種方法比較

方法 優點 限制
縫隙衝擊（Slit to Agar） 大體積、時間分布圖 設備大、難消毒
衝擊取樣（Impact） 可蒸汽滅菌、<10分鐘取1 m³ 笨重、難消毒
離心取樣（Centrifugal） 輕巧、可蒸汽滅菌、有氣體接頭 需特殊培養條
過濾法（Filtration） 低成本、多點監測友善 需確認濾材不抑菌

重點提示 Key Notes

明膠膜（Gelatin membrane filter）不適用壓縮氣體： 明膠遇到乾燥高壓氣流會脆化甚至破裂，造成取樣失敗或假陰性，這是一個必須避免的選材錯誤。在驗證取樣方法時，應明確確認所用濾材對目標菌種無抑制作用（菌回收率驗證, recovery validation）。

0.45 µm vs 0.2 µm： 環境微生物監測用0.45 µm（截留細菌），而不是0.2 µm——因為0.2 µm流阻大，取樣流量低，取樣時間過長。

比喻說明 Analogy

四種方法就像四種捕魚方式：衝擊法（撒大網）效率高但設備笨重；離心法（捕魚桶）輕巧靈活；過濾法（魚網）便宜可批量部署；液體衝擊法（魚缸過濾）可捕捉最脆弱的魚（vegetative cells），但玻璃設備易破。選擇哪種，取決於你要捕的「魚」種類和取樣點數量。

實務應用 CDMO Application

對CDMO來說，過濾法（filtration method）通常最實際：多客戶產品、多取樣點、需要靈活部署。但在無菌充填廠（aseptic filling facility）的N₂取樣，可能需要能蒸汽滅菌的衝擊取樣器——因為取樣本身不能污染系統，設備必須能完全滅菌，且取樣操作必須在RABS或隔離器環境中執行。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你要同時監測工廠的10個N₂使用點，預算有限。你會選擇哪種取樣方法？理由是什麼？
  2. 取樣方法驗證（method validation）中，「回收率」測試的目的是什麼？如何設計此測試？
6.3.2.3 Particulate Monitoring — 微粒監測

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

There are several methods and a variety of instrumentation available for detecting, sizing, and quantifying particulates in compressed gases.

Methods include laser particle counting, condensation nucleus counting coupled with scanning mobility particle sizing, differential mobility analysis, and membrane capture. The application of these methods is covered in ISO-8573-4:2001.

The laser particle counter method is commonly used for process gases, due to the moderate sample rate, relatively low cost, and low maintenance requirements. Care should be taken to avoid including moisture as droplets in particle counts and to ensure that the sample hose connecting the particle counter and the sample point does not contribute to the particle count. The tubing should be made of a smooth non-shedding material and as short as possible to avoid particle fallout. The connection to the sample port should avoid introducing exterior air or generation of particles.

Monitoring Process (high/low pressure)

Process gas systems usually supply gas at a flow or pressure that is too high for a particle counting instrument. The flow to the instrument should be restricted to prevent damage to the particle counter, as high pressure may damage the sensor. This is usually accomplished by using a device that supplies an appropriate flow rate to the particle counter while allowing the excess gas to be safely vented.

The monitoring process should ensure that the compressed gas flow to the particle counter does not fall below the point where outside air is introduced into the sample process. Sample points may supply process gas at flow or pressure below this critical threshold and a different technique should be used.

For such low flow/pressure sample points, the gas may be passed through a tube that would allow the pressure to diffuse while allowing the particle counter to sample the airflow without the gas stream being forced into the sensor. A qualification process should ensure that the particle counter is representatively counting particles in the gas stream.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

雷射微粒計數器（Laser Particle Counter, LPC）： 製程氣體微粒監測的主流技術。原理是讓氣體流過雷射光束，微粒散射光被偵測並計數/分級（通常為≥0.5 µm 和 ≥5.0 µm）。藥廠常用，符合ISO 8573-4和ISO 14644標準。

高壓取樣的挑戰： 製程氣體通常在6-8 bar以上輸送，但LPC的感測器設計在大氣壓附近，高壓氣體直接進入會損壞儀器。必須使用流量限制器（flow restrictor）或稀釋裝置（diluter），讓超量氣體安全排放。

重點提示 Key Notes — 水霧干擾計數

液態水滴（moisture droplets）在LPC中會被計為「微粒」，造成假性計數升高。這是一個系統性誤差來源，必須通過：

  • 確保氣體露點遠低於取樣環境溫度（避免凝結）
  • 取樣管線保溫或加熱
  • 使用疏水性材料的取樣管

低壓側的反向問題是：若氣體流量不足，環境空氣可能透過取樣孔進入（文氏效應），造成環境微粒污染取樣讀值——即「負壓引入外氣」現象。

比喻說明 Analogy

對LPC進行高壓製程氣體監測就像用一般血壓計量液壓機的壓力——你需要先用减壓閥把壓力降到儀器可接受範圍，讓超量壓力安全排出，儀器才能正確測量。取樣管線就像血壓計的充氣管，必須不脫落材質（non-shedding），否則管線自身的微粒會污染讀值。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的N₂供氣壓力為7 bar，環境溫度20°C，露點-40°C。在取樣時，你是否需要擔心水霧干擾微粒計數？為什麼？
  2. 取樣管線的材質選用有何要求？為什麼要「盡可能短」？
6.3.2.4 Moisture Monitoring — 水分監測

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Moisture in process gases is usually measured as dewpoint or pressure dewpoint. Methods usually include condensation devices, e.g.:

  • cooled mirror dewpoint hygrometers
  • electrolytic hygrometers
  • impedance hygrometers
  • polymer film relative humidity sensors

Quartz crystal microbalance and Surface Acoustic Wave (SAW) devices are usually too complex for pharmaceutical process gas applications.
