When using a hygrometer, the temperature and line pressure should be accounted for during dewpoint measurements. The instruments may be used in line for continuous monitoring or may be used to periodically monitor critical POUs.

The type used should be determined by the degree of accuracy required for downstream processes, maintenance and calibration schedules, costs, and equipment reliability.

Chilled Mirror Hygrometer

The chilled mirror is a widely used measurement device with an accurate field measured dewpoint over a wide range. A surface mirror or polished surface in contact with the gas stream is cooled until condensation forms. The temperature at which condensation is formed is the dewpoint. Chilled mirror hygrometers are negatively affected by particulates in the air stream and by hygroscopic inorganic salts and are considered an expensive instrument routinely used for process gases.

Electrolytic Hygrometer

This method is described in the PhEur and USP as a method for determining water in gases. The method is based on absorption of water by diphosphorus pentoxide to produce phosphoric acid as an electrical conductor. A voltage is applied to the water to produce electrolysis. The resulting current is proportional to the water content and based on Faraday's Law. The technique can provide stable and repeatable data but requires more attention to proper use to provide accurate results than other methods.

Impedance Hygrometers

These are typically ceramic, aluminum oxide, and silicon oxide based sensors. These sensors rely on a change in electrical property such as capacitance, impedance, or resistance of a porous layer in response to moisture in the gas stream. When properly calibrated and maintained, these instruments can provide good quality results. Calibration is required on a regular basis.

Polymer Film Relative Humidity (RH) Sensors

These sensors are similar to impedance hygrometers. These are constructed of a polymer with a hygroscopic dielectric material. As the water content changes, the dielectric properties change and the capacitance of the sensor changes to provide an electrical response. Hygrometers based on this principle offer relatively low cost and good quality results. These types of sensors are less susceptible to particulate contamination.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

露點（Dewpoint）vs 壓力露點（Pressure Dewpoint）：

  • 露點： 氣體在大氣壓下降溫至凝露的溫度，例如 -40°C dp
  • 壓力露點： 氣體在管線實際壓力（如7 bar）下的露點。同一批氣體，在高壓管線中的壓力露點比大氣露點高約20-25°C（因為壓縮使水分相對濃度升高）

比對規格書時必須注意：供應商通常標示大氣露點，但你的設備可能需要的是大氣壓下使用（降壓後），應正確換算。

四種水分監測技術比較

技術 原理 優點 限制
冷鏡（Chilled Mirror） 冷卻至凝露，測溫 精準、量程廣 貴、怕微粒
電解（Electrolytic） P₂O₅吸水、法拉第定律 PhEur/USP收載 操作要求高
阻抗（Impedance） 陶瓷/Al₂O₃電容變化 穩定、可在線 需定期校正
高分子薄膜（Polymer Film） 介電常數隨水分變化 低成本、耐微粒 量程相對窄

重點提示 Key Notes

露點監測的雙重意義：

  • 產品保護： 許多藥品（粉末、凍乾品）對水分敏感，氣體帶入水分會影響產品穩定性和CQA。
  • 系統保護： 高水分會造成配管腐蝕、過濾器堵塞、微生物繁殖。乾燥機失效→露點升高→下游問題連鎖。

電解法（P₂O₅法）被PhEur和USP收載為官方方法，代表在監管文件中具有最強的公信力，但操作技術要求高，廠方人員需培訓。

比喻說明 Analogy

冷鏡式露點計就像黃金標準的精密天秤——精確但昂貴且嬌貴。高分子薄膜傳感器就像電子秤——便宜、耐用、精度夠用，適合日常在線監測。選擇哪種，就像選擇計量工具：關鍵應用用天秤，日常監控用電子秤。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在CDMO的凍乾製程（lyophilization）中，腔體充填N₂前必須確認N₂露點達到規格（例如≤-40°C dp）。推薦策略：在N₂進入腔體的POU安裝在線阻抗式或高分子薄膜傳感器做連續監測，並定期用可攜式冷鏡式露點計進行比對校驗（calibration check）。若在線傳感器偏離，立即觸發OOS調查，並評估近期批次是否受影響。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的N₂乾燥機在6 bar壓力下的壓力露點規格為 -20°C pp dp。降壓到大氣壓後，理論大氣露點大約是多少？（提示：壓縮比約7倍，需換算）
  2. 為什麼電解式露點計「操作要求比其他方法更高」？你認為在校正計畫中需要特別注意什麼？
6.3.2.5 Hydrocarbons Monitoring — 碳氫化合物監測

原文內容 Original Text ISPE

Compressed air and other process gas systems intended for pharmaceutical applications should be designed and constructed with oil free compressors and hygienic piping. The installation of systems should include the concept of "build clean" where the equipment and piping are supplied in a clean condition and installed in a manner to prevent contamination.

The monitoring of hydrocarbons in compressed gas systems contributes to the qualification phase to ensure the piping is free of oils prior to use. When compressed air systems are appropriately designed and installed, the most significant risk to the system is the introduction of diesel (auto) fumes at the air intake for the compressor. Air intake for compressors should be considered in the design stage and care should be taken to avoid introduction of fumes into the system.

Depending on the air quality in the vicinity of a facility, compressed air quality may need to be monitored on an ongoing basis for high risk contaminants.

Two distinct methods may be identified based on the type of hydrocarbon component targeted:

  1. Total Hydrocarbon (THC)
  2. Total Volatile Hydrocarbons (TVHCs)

Total Hydrocarbon (THC) / Total Oil Mist: These may be detected and quantified using indicator tubes. The tubes contain chemicals that react with an introduced substance and change color. Oil indicator tubes are designed to monitor for specific oils and mists derived from a variety of mineral and synthetic oils. The detection limits are dependent on the volume of gas exposed to the tube medium and the specific type of oil. These tubes are not designed to detect hydrocarbon fumes.

Total Volatile Hydrocarbons (TVHCs): Volatile hydrocarbons are compounds that are either gases or liquids that can evaporate and act as a gas. The method does not detect oil mists. TVHCs may comprise many different types of volatile hydrocarbons; therefore, are measured and expressed as parts per million calculated as methane.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

THC vs TVHC：兩種不同的碳氫污染：

  • THC（Total Hydrocarbons / Oil Mist）： 液態油霧，來自壓縮機潤滑油、軸封洩漏等。即便使用無油壓縮機，進氣端的油霧污染也可能殘留。用指示管（indicator tubes）即時偵測。
  • TVHC（Total Volatile Hydrocarbons）： 揮發性氣態碳氫化合物，如汽油蒸氣、溶劑蒸氣，來自壓縮機進氣口周圍的環境空氣（停車場、鍋爐房、實驗室廢氣）。用ppb/ppm儀器偵測，以甲烷當量表達。

指示管（Indicator tubes）： 單次使用的比色試管，成本低、現場快速測定，但精度有限，適合定性/半定量用途。

重點提示 Key Notes — 進氣口設計

壓縮機進氣口位置是系統設計中最常被忽視的安全細節之一。正確選址原則：

  • 遠離停車場、裝卸區、發電機排氣管
  • 高度應高於地面（減少地面塵埃和廢氣吸入）
  • 設置空氣過濾器（空氣品質差的地區考慮活性炭前處理）
  • 定期採樣確認進氣口空氣品質

若廠址附近有新開幕的停車場或施工工地，需重新評估是否需要增加TVHC例行監測頻率。

比喻說明 Analogy

油霧（THC）就像肉眼幾乎看不到的廚房油煙，直接來自設備本身；揮發性碳氫化合物（TVHC）就像鄰居燒烤的煙——來自外部環境，從窗戶（進氣口）飄入。前者靠選用無油壓縮機預防，後者靠選對進氣口位置和持續環境監測。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在CDMO資格確認（qualification）流程中，壓縮空氣的碳氫化合物測試通常在IQ/OQ階段執行，目的是確認系統安裝時未引入油污。但ISPE指出：若廠房附近環境空氣品質差（如位於工業區、鄰近停車場），需要納入常規監測計畫，而非僅做一次性資格確認。這是CDMO在廠房選址或改建時需要預先評估的風險。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的廠剛完成壓縮空氣系統安裝，驗收測試顯示THC（油霧）讀值高於規格。可能的根本原因有哪些？如何逐一排除？
  2. TVHCs監測結果以「ppm calculated as methane」表達，這種表達方式有何意涵？當監測對象是複合有機溶劑蒸氣時，此方法有什麼局限性？

本章重點回顧 Chapter Summary

  • 管控系統三類： 壓縮空氣（廠方自有，露點控制切換）、鋼瓶（自動切換+BMS整合）、現場產氣（供應商控制，廠方需複製儀表管理校正）。設計階段即需規劃整合。
  • 壓力非CPP的ISPE立場： 幹管壓力是工程參數，真正的關鍵監測點在各POU入口，設備自帶的壓力開關才是關鍵儀表。
  • 品質等同原則： 製程氣體進入潔淨室，微粒和微生物品質必須≥所在室的靜態等級（Annex 1 / 21 CFR Part 210要求）。
  • 低露點不等於無菌： 乾燥可抑制微生物生長，但芽孢（endospores）在極乾環境下仍可長期存活。唯一可靠的屏障是0.2 µm滅菌級POU過濾器。
  • 取樣位置策略： 取樣應在最終過濾器上游進行，最長管路末端是最具代表性的風險點；過濾器下游取樣風險大，每次取樣都可能污染已滅菌流路。
  • 水分監測選型： 冷鏡（最精準但貴）、電解（PhEur/USP認可）、阻抗（穩定在線）、高分子薄膜（低成本、耐微粒）——根據應用精度和預算選擇；露點vs壓力露點需正確換算。
  • 碳氫化合物雙重風險： THC（油霧，來自設備）靠無油壓縮機和指示管監測；TVHC（揮發性碳氫，來自外部環境）靠進氣口選址和持續環境監測管控。
  • CDMO OOS連接： 任何製程氣體品質OOS事件都必須觸發偏差調查，評估批次衝擊，並決定放行、隔離或報廢——氣體品質數據是批次記錄的一部分。

Chapter 5: Risk Assessment, Final Design & O&M (Ch 7–9)

風險評估、最終設計與操作維護 | p81-p98

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases | p81–p98

本章學習目標

  • 理解品質風險管理 (QRM) 如何應用於製程氣體系統，以保障產品品質與病患安全
  • 掌握 FMEA 風險評估框架：風險識別、風險分析、風險評估與風險控制的四步驟循環
  • 了解工程移交文件包 (Engineering Turnover Package, ETOP) 的結構與查核重點
  • 熟悉氣體系統試運行 (Commissioning) 與裝置確效/操作確效 (IQ/OQ) 的差異與銜接關係
  • 掌握績效測試 (Performance Testing) 對各使用點 (POU) 氣體品質的驗收標準
  • 了解維護與校正計畫在 GMP 合規中的法規要求與最佳實務
Chapter 7 — Risk Assessment 風險評估
7.1 Introduction

原文內容 Original Text

A risk assessment process is normally part of the Quality Risk Management (QRM) effort. The Quality Risk Management process, as applied to a process gas system, should ensure the reliable delivery of gas meeting the specifications to POUs. The delivery system should not present a high risk of affecting defined quality attributes of the process gas supplied; therefore assuring suitability for the application for which the process gas is used.

This chapter follows the science- and risk-based principles described in ICH Q9, ASTM E2500-07, and the ISPE Guide on the Science and Risk-Based Approach for the Delivery of Facilities, Systems, and Equipment.

Risk management should reduce risks to an acceptable level. Complete elimination of risk is neither practical nor necessary. In a process gas system, sources of risks to product quality and patient safety include:

  • distribution system design
  • operation of system safety features
  • method of generation or source of a gas

In order to apply a science- and risk-based approach, a thorough understanding of the product/process requirements, gas generation/source attributes, and the storage and distribution system are required. The utilization of process knowledge and understanding, which considers both Critical Quality Attributes (CQAs) and Critical Process Parameters (CPPs), will help to optimize the design of a new gas system, or revisions to existing systems.

Relevant CQAs and CPPs should be defined. They will typically be determined by the application for which a process gas is used.

Table 7.1 — Typical Quality Attributes for a Process Gas

# Quality Attribute Specification / Guideline
1 Gas Purity Applicable for inert gases such as Nitrogen, as per USP/EU Monograph
2 Moisture (Water Aerosols or Vapor) Non-sterile or sterile applications — NMT 2.5 g/kg (−40°F/−40°C dewpoint)
3 Hydrocarbons (Oil Content) NMT 0.5 mg/m³
4 Other Chemical Impurities (as applicable) Based on generation technology and/or USP/EU Monograph
5 Microbial Count (Non-sterile Applications) Guideline limits based on product bioburden; typical NMT 5 cfu/m³
6 Microbial Count (Sterile Applications) Per viable particle requirements for Grade area (Grade A, A/B, B, or C)
7 Particle Count (Viable and Non-viable) Typically equal to the at-rest condition of the area served

The primary drivers of a process gas system's design are: (1) capacity, (2) usage, (3) output quality. A risk assessment should identify risk resulting from specific and critical aspects of a proposed design. Identified critical aspects should be the focus of the subsequent verification effort.

A risk assessment may be simplified for existing systems (i.e., legacy systems), where system functionality and capacity have been demonstrated during the period of use, and the system operating range, performance capabilities, etc., are known.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — QRM 與製程氣體

品質風險管理 Quality Risk Management (QRM)：源自 ICH Q9，是一套系統化識別、評估、控制品質風險的方法論。應用於氣體系統時，核心目標是確保每個使用點 (POU) 都能穩定接收符合規格的氣體。

風險的三個來源：設計缺陷、安全系統失效、氣體來源問題——這三者涵蓋了整個氣體系統的生命週期。

CQA vs CPP 在氣體系統中：CQA 如露點、含油量、微生物計數；CPP 如壓力、流量、溫度。QRM 的本質是保護這些關鍵屬性不受風險影響。

比喻說明 Analogy

把氣體系統的風險評估想像成醫院感染管控計畫 (CCS)：你無法消除所有細菌，但你可以識別高風險區域（手術室 vs 走廊），設定對應的控制措施，並持續監控。製程氣體 QRM 也是如此——不追求零風險，而是將風險降至可接受水準。

重點提示 Key Note

Table 7.1 的 CQA 列表非常實用：無菌應用 (Sterile) 的微生物計數要求必須符合所服務潔淨室等級的環境監控標準，例如 Grade A 區域的氣體就需達到 Grade A 的粒子規格。這是 CDMO 稽核中常被查核的重點。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一條氮氣管線同時服務 Grade B 充填區和 Grade C 物料準備區，CQA 規格應以哪個等級為準？理由為何？
  2. 「完全消除風險既不實際也非必要」這句話的含義是什麼？在 CDMO 的商業環境中如何平衡？
7.2 Quality Risk Management for Process Gas Systems

原文內容 Original Text

The Quality Risk Management approach should be applied throughout the life cycle of a process gas system and is described within this Guide to support:

  • development of the User Requirements
  • development and review of the process gas system design
  • determination of the scope of verification testing activities (commissioning, installation, functional, and performance testing)
  • determination of the optimum scope and scale of a calibration program
  • determination of appropriate preventive maintenance programs
  • determination of the scope and frequency of routine monitoring programs
  • to ensure assumptions made during the risk assessment were appropriate during system operation

Risk management provides an opportunity to generate a rationale for scaling activities appropriately. Results may be used to justify reduction, increase, or the omission or inclusion of an activity.

The risk-based approach activities should be appropriately resourced and focused. Effort and time devoted to a risk management process should be commensurate with the potential impact on the supported business process.

The principles used for QRM may be used to review other (risk) areas such as:

  • Environment, Health, and Safety (EHS)
  • identification of revalidation scope and frequency for existing systems
  • assessment of the potential impact of proposed changes

Though, there is usually a desire to keep quality related aspects separate to facilitate future audit.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — QRM 的生命週期應用

QRM 不是一次性的文件，而是貫穿氣體系統整個生命週期的持續活動：從 URS 撰寫、設計審查、試運行範圍決定、校正頻率設定、預防性維護計畫，到例行監控頻率調整，每個環節都由風險評估結果驅動。

重點提示 — 資源投入與風險成比例

「投入的心力應與業務影響成比例」——這句話對 CDMO 特別重要。直接接觸產品的 Grade A 氣體系統，比工廠公用動力用壓縮空氣值得投入更多 QRM 資源。不要在低風險系統上過度確效，也不要在高風險系統上省略關鍵步驟。

比喻說明 Analogy

QRM 就像醫院的「分類系統 (Triage)」：急診室依病情嚴重程度分配醫療資源，而不是每個病人都用最高規格治療。氣體系統 QRM 也是如此——讓高風險的環節獲得充足驗證資源，低風險環節減少不必要的確效活動。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在 CDMO 接受新客戶委託時，常需要評估既有氣體系統是否適用於客戶產品。QRM 結果直接影響：是否需要追加確效測試、哪些 POU 需要加裝 POU 過濾器、預防性維護計畫是否需要調整。這些決策若有風險評估支撐，面對客戶稽核時更具說服力。

7.3 Risk Assessment Process — 風險評估流程

原文內容 Original Text

7.3.1 Initiating a Risk Assessment

Determining the risks associated with a process gas system requires an understanding of factors such as:

  • site/organization standards and specifications
  • regulatory requirements
  • project approach (contracts, methods, timelines)
  • process/product requirements — used to determine required specification and potential risks
  • anticipated system design specifications: areas served, layout of distribution, environmental conditions at POU
  • system boundaries (what falls within scope)

For existing process gas distribution systems (legacy systems), factors include:

  • whether a single gas distribution system is shared between GMP and non-GMP applications
  • physical boundaries in place (non-return valves, filters) segregating critical and non-critical sections
  • available historical data (deviations, monitoring trends, performed changes)
  • design specifications: initial cleaning and commissioning specifications

The Risk Assessment process involves:

  1. Risk Identification / Hazard Severity
  2. Risk Analysis
  3. Risk Evaluation

7.3.2 Risk Identification / Hazard Severity

Risk identification involves the systematic use of data to identify hazards that could affect CPPs, CQAs, or critical aspects of a process gas system. Potential risks to typical product CQAs from a compressed air system include:

  • hydrocarbon (oil vapor and particulate) content
  • increased moisture levels
  • viable particulates
  • non-viable particulates (other than hydrocarbon)
  • gaseous impurities
  • process gas mix-up (e.g., connection of oxygen container to nitrogen distribution system)
  • reverse flow

Risk Controls may include: (1) system design features, (2) procedural controls.

7.3.3 Risk Analysis

Risk analysis is the estimation of the risk associated with identified hazards. It is the qualitative or quantitative process of linking the severity of a hazard, likelihood of occurrence, and the ability to detect harm.

A phased approach may be employed: initially using a qualitative assessment to differentiate low risks from medium to high risks, followed by quantitative scoring of medium-to-high risks.

7.3.4 Risk Evaluation

Risk evaluation compares the identified and analyzed risk against given risk criteria. Risk evaluations consider the strength of evidence for the three fundamental questions:

  1. What might go wrong?
  2. What is the likelihood (probability) it will go wrong?
  3. What are the consequences (severity)?

Outcomes may be expressed qualitatively ("high," "medium," "low") or quantitatively (numeric ranking). Ranking systems should be pre-defined.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — FMEA 三要素

氣體系統風險評估通常採用 FMEA (失效模式與影響分析) 架構，三個評分維度：

  • 嚴重性 Severity (S)：失效後果對產品品質/病患安全的影響程度
  • 發生可能性 Occurrence (O)：在現有控制措施下，風險事件發生的機率
  • 可偵測性 Detection (D)：在危害發生後，被偵測到的難易度

風險優先數 (RPN) = S × O × D，用於排序需要優先控制的失效模式。

典型壓縮空氣系統 FMEA 範例

失效模式          S  O  D  RPN  控制措施
壓縮機失效        4  2  2   16  備用機組+壓力警報
過濾器堵塞        3  3  2   18  差壓監控+定期更換
水分突破          4  2  1    8  露點連續監測+高警報
N₂中混入O₂        5  1  1    5  止回閥+氣體分析儀
油蒸氣污染        4  2  2   16  無油壓縮機+活性碳過濾
微生物污染        4  1  3   12  POU過濾器+微生物監控

S/O/D 評分 1-5（5=最高嚴重/最常發生/最難偵測）

重點提示 — 氣體混用風險

Process gas mix-up（氣體混用）是評分嚴重性最高的風險之一：若氧氣容器錯接至氮氣分配系統，可能造成爆炸或產品氧化。控制措施包括：使用不同接頭規格、明確的顏色標示、接管前的 ID 測試程序，以及最終的 GC 分析確認。這在 CDMO 環境中是一個必須寫進 SOP 的管控項目。

比喻說明 Analogy

三步驟風險評估（識別→分析→評估）就像醫院的病例診斷程序：先列出所有可能症狀（識別），評估每個症狀的嚴重程度與發生機率（分析），最後決定是否達到需要治療的門檻（評估）。不是每個風險都需要立即處置，但每個高 RPN 的風險都必須有對應的控制措施。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 在進行既有（legacy）氣體系統的風險評估時，歷史數據能發揮什麼作用？相比新系統，評估範圍會如何調整？
  2. 「逆流 (reverse flow)」風險在什麼情況下最容易發生？應採取哪些設計控制措施？
7.4–7.6 Risk Control, Communication & Review

原文內容 Original Text

7.4 Risk Control

Risk control includes decision making either to reduce risks or accept them, or both. The purpose of risk control is to reduce the risk to an acceptable level. The amount of effort applied to risk control should be proportional to the significance of the risk.

Risk control addresses the following questions:

  • Is the risk above an acceptable level?
  • What can be done to reduce or eliminate the risk?
  • What is the appropriate balance of risk likelihood/controls?
  • Are new risks introduced as a result of the controls being applied?

Risk reduction follows a hierarchy:

  1. reduction through design changes
  2. reduction through procedural change

Potential for New or Increased Risk: The implementation of risk reduction measures can introduce new risks into a system or increase the significance of existing risks. After implementation, the results of a risk assessment should be reassessed.

Risk acceptance is a decision to accept risk. Risk acceptance can be formal (documented acceptance of residual risk) or passive (residual risks not specified).

7.5 Risk Assessment Communication

Risk communication should ensure that the results of a risk assessment are shared with relevant team members, the system owner, and senior management. Communication can occur at any stage of the risk management process.

The output and result of the Quality Risk Management process should be appropriately documented and communicated. The risk assessment report may be used to assist in the definition of the scope of the required system verification.

The scores given in the risk assessment are normally based on the assumption that the controls defined are in place and operational; to accept the result of the risk assessment, the operation of the design controls should be verified and the procedural controls defined should be confirmed as being in place, with the relevant staff trained on the procedures.

7.6 Risk Review

The risk assessment should be periodically reviewed to ensure that the scoring used reflects the operational experience with the system. The period between these re-evaluations should be defined and based on potential risk and the novelty of the system.

A periodic review may also be invoked by events such as changes in the system use or system modifications.

Data gathered during a risk assessment may be used to identify opportunities to decrease GMP risks. The results may be useful for product review, inspections, audits, or root cause failure investigations.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 風險控制的層級優先順序

ISPE 明確規定風險控制的優先順序：

  1. 設計變更（最優先）：從根本消除風險來源，例如改用無油壓縮機消除油污染風險
  2. 程序控制（次之）：透過 SOP、人員訓練、警報設定等軟性控制降低風險

這個優先順序與 EU GMP Annex 1 的污染控制策略 (CCS) 設計原則完全一致。

重點提示 — 風險評估的前提條件

關鍵洞察：「風險評估分數假設控制措施已到位並運作中」——這意味著若驗收報告批准了風險評估，就等同於確認控制措施確實在運行。這是 CDMO 在設施稽核中必須能夠舉證的：你的 RPN 分數有多低，你的控制措施就需要有多健全的執行證據。

比喻說明 — 風險接受 vs 風險降低

風險接受就像保險決策：你不會為了每一個可能的意外都買保險，但對高金額損失的風險（如氣體汙染批次報廢），你一定要有明確的保障措施。「被動接受」（從未定義殘餘風險）是不可接受的做法，就像開車不買任何保險。

實務應用 — 定期風險審查的觸發條件

CDMO 實務中，以下事件應觸發風險評估審查：

  • 系統改建或管線變更（變更控制啟動）
  • 新產品引入，改變了 POU 的使用目的
  • 偏差事件或重複性 OOS 結果
  • 定期（如每年）審查週期到期
  • 監管機構視察後的改善要求

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若為了降低壓縮空氣含油風險而加裝額外過濾器，可能引入什麼新風險？
  2. 風險評估報告如何幫助定義系統確效 (Qualification) 的範圍？請舉一個具體例子。
Chapter 8 — Final Design, Commissioning & Qualification 最終設計、試運行與確效
8.1–8.2 Introduction & Engineering Turnover Package (ETOP)

原文內容 Original Text

8.1 Introduction

This section describes the installation, functional, and performance testing processes for process gas systems. These processes should demonstrate that a process gas system is "suitable for its intended purpose."

For process gas systems supplying product or product primary containers, performance testing should demonstrate that the supplied process gas quality meets the gas specifications required at the POUs.

Risk assessments may be used to develop an initial testing and ongoing performance monitoring strategy. Utilization of the results of a risk assessment can assist in optimizing system design, and define critical aspects of the system performance that require verification.

"Process gas systems are intrinsically different from water and steam systems and any comparison with the requirements for these systems should be avoided. (From a quality perspective it is not usually critical to test for drainability/sloping, dead legs, Materials of Construction (MoC), or surface roughness.)"

8.2 Engineering Turnover Package (ETOP)

The Engineering Turnover Package (ETOP) is considered one of the main construction deliverables. The ETOP is composed of three sections:

1. Construction Manager's Section — should contain:

  • a copy of the basis of design (User Requirements)
  • a set of issue for construction drawings and specifications
  • a copy of the submittals
  • a copy of any relevant permits
  • a change record history
  • a Request for Information (RFI) history
  • the construction quality check records, including third party inspections where appropriate
  • a copy of the final (closed out) punch list
  • the formal contractors certificate of completion

2. Installation Contractor's Section — should contain:

  • "red line" or "as built" record drawings and specifications
  • equipment list and instrument list
  • copies of calibration certificates or certificates of conformity
  • copies of warranties
  • welders certification or equivalent
  • weld procedures or equivalent
  • calibration certificates for construction equipment used
  • system and equipment operating and maintenance manuals
  • material certification/purchase orders and test records

3. Commissioning Section — should contain:

  • walk down "as built" record drawings
  • verified equipment list and instrument list
  • commissioning report for the equipment/system/controls
  • initial system test records

Monitoring the construction and completion of a project using the ETOP throughout the project to ensure timely and competent completion can save both time and money at the end of a project.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — ETOP 的角色

工程移交文件包 Engineering Turnover Package (ETOP) 是從「施工完成」到「確效開始」的橋樑文件。它的三個組成部分對應三個不同的責任方：

  • 施工管理者：確保設計意圖被正確執行
  • 安裝承包商：提供設備安裝的完整證明文件
  • 試運行團隊：記錄系統初始性能基準

ETOP 是 IQ 確效的主要資料來源——確效工程師從這裡取得圖面、設備清單、校正記錄，與現場實際狀況進行比對。

重點提示 — 常見稽核發現

CDMO 在稽核中最常被查到的 ETOP 問題：

  • P&ID 缺失或版本不一致："As-built" 圖面與實際管路不符，尤其是後期的系統改建未更新 P&ID
  • 校正紀錄缺漏：儀表安裝合格證明或出廠校正書未歸入 ETOP
  • 焊接紀錄不完整：高純度氣體管路的焊工資格證書遺失
  • Punch list 未完全關閉：遺留的待改善項目在移交時未被記錄

比喻說明 Analogy

ETOP 就像新房交屋時的驗屋報告：建商必須提供完整的施工圖、材料規格書、水電管線圖，以及所有試驗合格證明。沒有完整的交屋文件，就算房子蓋好了，你也不知道裡面埋的是什麼材質的管線。氣體系統的 ETOP 邏輯完全相同——它是你對系統「來歷清白」的法律憑證。

重點提示 — 氣體系統 vs 水系統的差異

ISPE 明確指出：氣體系統確效不需要測試排放坡度、死角、材質表面粗糙度等水系統的常規項目。這是因為氣體不會積水，微生物無法在乾燥氣體中繁殖。CDMO 的確效協議書不應盲目套用水系統的 IQ 查核清單於氣體系統。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若在安裝確效 (IQ) 期間發現 P&ID 與實際安裝有差異，應如何處理？這會影響確效進度嗎？
  2. ETOP 中的「Commissioning Section」與正式的 IQ/OQ 文件有何不同？哪些資料可以直接引用？
8.3 Commissioning 試運行

原文內容 Original Text

The scope and extent of the commissioning activities for a process gas system depends on the system specifications and design.

Process gas systems should be commissioned according to Good Engineering Practice (GEP) and documented evidence that the system is installed and operates in accordance with the design should be provided. As part of commissioning, calibration of instruments should be verified. The correct setting and function of the system safety devices should be checked.

Commissioning documents may be pre-approved by an organization's engineering group (relevant SMEs). For large projects, approvals may include a project manager. Commissioning documents do not normally require pre-approval by the quality unit.

Pre-start up or start up readiness checks — typical tests for Compressors and Air Dryers:

  • record of all cable tests (continuity, insulation)
  • record of all grounding (earth) testing
  • record of fuse ratings/overload settings
  • point to point wiring tests (where applicable)
  • instrument and loop calibration records as specified
  • sequence of operation testing including interlocks and alarms
  • system auto/manual operation; dryer switchover (if dual tower)
  • installation, operation, and maintenance manuals availability
  • parts list, spare parts lists, and consumables lists
  • "as built" drawings (E&I diagrams, P&ID, layout)
  • certification from appropriate organizations (e.g., CAGI)

Typical tests for Distribution System:

  • material certification/purchase orders, inspection certificates, welding records
  • pipe work pressure testing records including insurance or inspection authority reports
  • record of pipe work cleaning and purging
  • pipe work passivation records (if applicable)
  • filter certification
  • instrument and loop calibration records as specified
  • sequence of operation testing: pressure control, economizer, vaporizer switchover, telemetry testing
  • "as built" drawings (E&I diagrams, P&ID, layout)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — Commissioning vs Qualification 的分界

這是製藥工程中一個關鍵的概念邊界：

  • 試運行 Commissioning：由工程部門主導，依 GEP 執行，證明系統按設計安裝與運作。不需要 QA 事前批准。
  • 確效 Qualification (IQ/OQ/PQ)：由品保/確效部門主導，依 GMP 法規要求執行，需要 QA 事前批准協議書。

ISPE 的「Science and Risk-Based Approach」(ASTM E2500) 框架允許充分利用試運行資料支援確效，避免重複測試，節省成本與時間。

比喻說明 Analogy

試運行就像新車出廠前的品管測試：工廠測試煞車、引擎、電氣系統，確保一切按規格運作。而確效（GMP 環境）則像醫療器材上市前的臨床驗證：在實際使用環境中，依照預定規格進行有文件記錄的驗證，最終由品保部門批准放行。

重點提示 — 壓力測試與清洗紀錄

管路壓力測試 (pressure testing) 與吹掃/清洗紀錄 (purging) 是試運行的核心項目。對於高純度氣體系統：

  • 壓力測試通常在 1.5 倍最高工作壓力下進行，確認管路完整性
  • 系統在性能測試前必須充分吹掃，以去除施工殘留物（金屬碎屑、焊接殘渣）
  • 鈍化 (passivation) 紀錄適用於不鏽鋼高純度氣體管路

實務應用 — CDMO 專案管理角度

CDMO 在承接新廠建置或擴產項目時，建議在合約中明確規定 ETOP 的交付要求與時間點，並指定哪些試運行數據將被納入確效協議引用。這樣可以有效縮短從設施完工到第一批產品放行的時間軸。

8.4 Installation and Operational Tests (IQ/OQ) 裝置確效與操作確效

原文內容 Original Text

Installation and operational tests are usually conducted in accordance with the design specifications and contracts, with the results documented in the commissioning document. The organization's requirements for engineering documentation should be specified, so that quality departments are able to use the engineering document to provide the evidence of installation and operation to meet the design specifications.

A typical P&ID walk down procedure:

  • Obtain the copy of the latest revision of the P&ID with all changes incorporated, usually as construction redline drawings.
  • Perform a walk down of the P&ID, red-lining it to reflect the as-built condition. Use an indelible ink pen of the following colors:
    • Red: indicate additions or corrections
    • Green: indicate deletions
    • Black: enter comments or notes
    • Yellow highlighter: show what sections have been verified
  • Highlight all equipment, valves, instruments, lines, etc., to indicate installation per latest P&ID.
  • Highlight tag numbers on the P&ID to confirm correct tagging.
  • Upon completion, the person performing the walk down signs and dates "Verified by" on the P&ID.
  • The system owner reviews the red-lined P&ID and signs "Reviewed by".
  • Place items such as missing tags, incomplete insulation, etc., on the Punch list.
  • Review the changes and errors and decide if the installation is acceptable or if errors need correction (punch list items).

Note that for compressed air systems, where the compressor/dryer capacities are critical, an independent certificate (e.g., a CAGI certificate) may be required as part of the specification.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — P&ID Walk Down 的意義

P&ID 現場查核 (Walk Down) 是 IQ 的核心活動之一。其目的是確認現場實際安裝與設計圖面完全一致，並將所有差異記錄在「紅線圖」上，最終決定這些差異是否可接受，或需要列入 Punch List 要求承包商改正。

對 CDMO 而言，IQ 確效協議通常引用試運行期間完成的 P&ID walk down 記錄，而不需要重複執行相同的步驟——這正是科學風險導向確效的效益。

重點提示 — Punch List 的管理

Punch List 是一份「待解決問題清單」。確效的前提是所有影響系統功能的 Punch List 項目必須關閉 (closed out)。允許保留的 open items 通常只限於對系統性能無影響的外觀或行政性問題，且必須有書面的風險評估支撐。稽核中常見的問題是確效報告批准時仍有未關閉的重要 Punch List 項目。

IQ 查核清單重點項目

裝置確效 (IQ) 查核內容：
□ P&ID walk down 完成並簽署
□ 設備清單與現場實物核對
□ 儀表清單與校正憑證核對
□ 材質合格證明 (Mill Certificates)
□ 焊接紀錄與焊工資格
□ 管路壓力測試紀錄
□ 吹掃/清洗紀錄
□ Punch List 全數關閉
□ SOP 與維護手冊到位
□ 人員訓練記錄到位

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. P&ID walk down 發現某個安全閥的位置與圖面不符，但功能相同。這算不算需要列入 Punch List 的問題？
  2. CAGI 認證對壓縮機的意義是什麼？為何這可能需要作為規格要求的一部分？
8.5–8.6 Performance Testing & Acceptance and Release 性能測試與放行

原文內容 Original Text

8.5 Performance Testing

Initial system performance testing and ongoing monitoring may be performed by an organization's quality unit. Performance testing should demonstrate correct system functionality under procedural control. This usually takes place after the commissioning tests have demonstrated that the system is capable of performing to meet the design specifications.

A test plan for verifying the system performance with a supporting rationale should be included in the performance testing document. Performance testing is normally performed in two phases:

  1. an initial set of tests to confirm installed system performance and release the system for use
  2. an ongoing test plan to provide assurance that the critical performance parameters are being maintained (typically part of the routine monitoring program)

Performance testing usually consists of sampling for the quality attributes at each POU under normal operating conditions. Each POU should be sampled at least three consecutive times over a defined period and the data obtained should be evaluated for compliance with predefined acceptance criteria.

Initially monitoring of the POUs may be performed at more frequent intervals to further demonstrate adequate system performance over time. Once sufficient confidence of correct system performance has been acquired, based upon a statistically representative data set, the monitoring frequency may be decreased appropriately.

8.6 Acceptance and Release

Completion of the verification phase should include a verification (qualification) summary report which states whether the system is fit for its intended purpose and can be released for use. This report should confirm that:

  • A system has been installed according to the design specification.
  • Instrumentation is calibrated in accordance with the design specifications.
  • The system operates in accordance with the design specifications.
  • Risk controls identified during any risk assessments are in place and operating as specified.
  • The system performance testing results complied with the acceptance criteria.
  • Operating and maintenance procedures are established.

Approval of the verification (qualification) summary report by the system owner, engineering department, and validation/quality representative is normally considered confirmation that the system is suitable for intended use and is released for operational use.

Ownership should be transferred from the project team to the operations/engineering departments. Once the report is approved, formal Quality Assurance (QA) change and deviation management should be applied to the system.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — OQ 與 PQ 的銜接

氣體系統的「Performance Testing」相當於傳統確效架構中的 OQ（操作確效） 和 PQ（性能確效） 的組合：

  • 類似 OQ：確認系統在規格範圍內運作，如壓力控制、流量、警報功能
  • 類似 PQ：在各 POU 採樣確認氣體品質符合規格（露點、粒子、微生物、油含量）

「至少三次連續採樣」的要求是統計可信度的最低標準，對於新系統或高風險應用，應考慮增加取樣次數。

重點提示 — OQ 失敗情境管理

CDMO 實務中，若性能測試出現 OOS 結果（如 N₂ 沖洗後 O₂ 分析儀讀值超標），標準調查流程：

  1. 確認儀器校正狀態是否正常（排除量測誤差）
  2. 延長沖洗時間並重新取樣
  3. 檢查接頭與閥件的密封完整性（排除外氣滲入）
  4. 確認系統清洗/吹掃紀錄是否充分
  5. 評估是否需要調整 OQ 接受標準（需有科學依據）
  6. 所有調查步驟必須書面記錄

重點提示 — 移交後的 QA 管控

確效報告核准後，系統正式移交至運營部門，所有後續的：系統修改、儀表校正窗口變更、過濾器規格變更、操作參數調整，都必須通過 正式變更管控 (Change Control) 處理。這是稽核查核的高頻區域，特別是「系統在確效後有沒有被修改但沒有通知 QA」的問題。

實務應用 — 確效報告的批准結構

標準的確效摘要報告批准三方：系統負責人 (System Owner)、工程部門代表、品保/確效代表。三方簽署等同於正式宣告系統符合 GMP 用途。CDMO 應確保批准層級與客戶期望一致，尤其是委外客戶提供確效策略時。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若壓縮空氣系統有 20 個 POU，是否每個都需要取樣三次？或者可以依風險分層選取代表性 POU？
  2. 績效測試通過後，監控頻率可以降低的依據是什麼？需要什麼統計工具或數據量支撐？
Chapter 9 — Operation and Maintenance 日常操作與維護
9.1 Maintenance 維護管理

原文內容 Original Text

The principles described in the ISPE Good Practice Guide: Maintenance and the ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: A Risk-Based Approach to Calibration Management should be applied to process gas systems.

Equipment suppliers should provide general recommendations and training for equipment operation and maintenance, including the change frequency for worn components.

The effect of the financial value of product and equipment failure on the maintenance program should be assessed. The requirement for an equipment log should be considered (CFR 211.68/ Eudralex Volume 4 Annex 1).

9.1.1 Factors for Consideration in a Maintenance Program

9.1.1.1 Risk Assessment Results
The results of a risk assessment should be reviewed to determine their effect on the maintenance strategy. Where maintenance is identified as a control, the scope and frequency of maintenance activities should be commensurate with the risk.

9.1.1.2 Changing of Filters
General filters are normally industrial grade; their life should be defined by the designer or equipment supplier based on their usage. Filters should be changed regularly; the frequency change may depend on system usage.

Use of differential pressure as a solitary indication for filter changing may not be a good practice, unless the differential pressure is monitored at a known gas flow rate.

Initial system performance monitoring should include one maintenance cycle for the filters as a minimum.

Higher grade or POU filters should have a defined change and test routine, particularly where the filter is the critical component forming the interface between a non-GMP and GMP process gas system.

9.1.1.3 Cleaning of the Equipment
Equipment should be kept clean to facilitate early recognition of any leaks and provide a visual assurance of the degree of care provided to critical equipment.

9.1.1.4 Functional Testing of the Equipment
Where equipment is provided in a duty standby configuration, the automatic switchover should be checked routinely. Routine maintenance should be thorough, particularly of equipment that may impact on the CQAs of process gases, e.g., automatic drain valves. Regional regulations may require routine testing and inspection of safety equipment, pressure relief valves, and storage vessels, etc.

9.1.1.5 Leak Testing and Energy and Usage Monitoring
Process gas systems should be tested for leaks. This may be performed using ultrasonic equipment during system operation or using a pressure decay test. Monitoring can identify significant changes in energy consumption or gas usage by a system.

9.1.2 System Trending
Aspects that can be recorded and trended include:

  • oil consumption of a lubricated compressor
  • power consumption of a gas system
  • gas consumption
  • system pressure
  • number of system stop/starts
  • system loading/unloading patterns

Techniques such as oil analysis and vibration monitoring should be considered. Periodic monitoring of equipment vibration can identify significant changes that may indicate equipment wear or failure.

9.1.2.1 Spares Holding
A strategy for defining spare parts and consumables inventory should be established. This should consider the availability of spare parts locally, and delivery times for key components. A stock holding and reorder level should be defined and reviewed periodically against usage history.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 預防性維護 (PM) 的法規依據

EU GMP (Eudralex Vol.4 Annex 1) 和 FDA 21 CFR 211.68 都要求對製藥生產設備維護設備日誌 (equipment log)。氣體系統屬於「直接影響製程的公用設施」，因此其預防性維護計畫必須：

  • 有書面 PM 程序 (SOP)
  • 依時程執行並有執行紀錄
  • PM 項目的設定有科學/風險依據
  • 任何 PM 項目的更動需通過變更管控

重點提示 — 過濾器更換的變更管控

POU 過濾器是 GMP 與非 GMP 氣體系統之間的關鍵屏障。過濾器規格（孔徑、材質、廠商）的任何變更都必須經過正式的變更管控 (Change Control) 處理，包括：

  • 影響評估（是否影響 CQA？）
  • 必要時重新進行過濾完整性測試
  • 更新 PM 程序與設備清單
  • 通知下游使用部門

「單純更換相同規格的消耗品」通常不需要完整的變更管控，但需要有清楚的材料核准清單 (Approved Supplier List) 定義什麼是「相同規格」。

重點提示 — 差壓不是唯一的換濾指標

ISPE 明確指出：不應單獨用差壓作為換濾指標，除非差壓是在已知流量條件下量測的。原因：若流量降低（例如實際使用量減少），差壓也會降低，可能給出「過濾器狀態良好」的假象，即使過濾器已達壽命終點。建議結合時間基準 (time-based) 和差壓雙重標準執行換濾計畫。

系統趨勢監控的意義

監控趨勢項目      異常訊號         可能原因
油耗增加          超出基準 30%+    壓縮機密封件磨損
電力消耗上升      持續增加趨勢     壓縮機效率降低/過濾器堵塞
氣體消耗異常      突然大幅增加     系統洩漏
啟停次數增加      超出設計頻率     壓縮機容量不足/洩漏
振動值上升        超出基準值       軸承磨損/機械失衡

趨勢監控 = 預防性維護的眼睛
早期發現 → 計畫性停機維修
晚期發現 → 緊急停機 + 潛在生產損失

實務應用 — CDMO 備件管理

備件庫存策略對 CDMO 的生產連續性至關重要。POU 過濾器、露點感應器的更換元件、壓縮機密封套件——這些「關鍵備件」的交期若超過 4–6 週，就應納入安全庫存計畫，並定期審查使用歷史更新再訂購點 (reorder point)。避免因備件斷料造成計畫外的氣體系統停機。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若一個工廠的壓縮空氣系統振動監控數值在過去 30 天持續上升 15%，應該如何回應？需要啟動哪些程序？
  2. 備用壓縮機（standby）的自動切換功能，在維護計畫中應如何驗證？多久驗證一次比較合適？
9.2 Calibration 校正管理

原文內容 Original Text

A calibration strategy should be defined during the system design. This should consider the features of the specific design, the reliability, function, and likely failure modes of sensors. Equipment suppliers usually can provide advice on calibration methods and frequencies.

The results of a risk assessment should be reviewed to determine their effect on the calibration strategy. Where alarms or instrumentation data are identified as a control, the scope and frequency of calibration activities should be commensurate with the risk.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念 — 風險導向的校正策略

ISPE 強調：校正策略必須由風險評估結果驅動。實務上，氣體系統儀表依重要性分層：

  • 產品關鍵 (Product Critical)：POU 露點感應器、O₂ 分析儀、微生物取樣設備 → 嚴格校正頻率（如每 6 個月）+ 校正失敗即啟動調查
  • 製程關鍵 (Process Critical)：系統壓力感應器、流量計 → 標準校正週期（如每年）
  • 非關鍵 (Non-Critical)：工程用壓力錶、非 GMP 區域儀表 → 延長校正間隔或目視檢查替代

比喻說明 Analogy

校正策略就像定期健康檢查的頻率：心臟病高風險患者每 3 個月一次、一般人每年一次、年輕健康的人可能 2–3 年一次。你不會讓所有人都做一樣頻率的檢查，而是依據「若這個指標出錯，後果有多嚴重？」來決定檢查頻率。氣體系統儀表校正邏輯完全相同。

重點提示 — 校正失敗的影響評估

當一個關鍵儀表校正失敗（讀值超出允許誤差），CDMO 必須：

  1. 立即隔離該儀表，避免繼續使用錯誤讀值做出決策
  2. 評估在上次校正合格日期至今，使用該儀表讀值做出的所有放行決定
  3. 若有批次在此期間放行，啟動回顧性偏差調查 (retrospective deviation)
  4. 確認是設備問題還是程序問題，並採取 CAPA

這個流程的嚴謹度直接體現了 GMP 對於量測系統管控的要求。

關鍵氣體系統儀表校正矩陣示例

儀表類型          重要性分類    校正頻率    校正標準
露點感應器(POU)   產品關鍵      6個月       NIST 可追溯基準
O₂分析儀(N₂系統) 產品關鍵      6個月       認證標準氣體
系統壓力傳送器    製程關鍵      12個月      校正氣壓計
流量計(用量監控)  製程關鍵      12個月      NIST 可追溯流量標準
壓縮機出口壓力錶  非關鍵        24個月      目視+功能檢查
工廠用壓力錶      非關鍵        24個月      比對法

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若氮氣系統的 O₂ 分析儀在校正時發現讀值偏低 0.2%（實際 O₂ 濃度比顯示值高），這對於過去 3 個月的氮氣品質放行記錄有什麼影響？
  2. 設備供應商建議每 12 個月校正一次露點感應器，但風險評估將其評為「產品關鍵」，你應該採用哪個頻率？理由為何？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary — Chapters 7–9

  • Ch7 QRM 原則：品質風險管理應貫穿氣體系統整個生命週期，從 URS 到日常維護。風險評估的三步驟（識別→分析→評估）是 FMEA 的核心架構，ICH Q9 是基礎法規參考。
  • Ch7 氣體系統常見失效模式：壓縮機失效、過濾器堵塞、水分突破、O₂ 滲入 N₂、氣體混用——每個都需要有對應的設計控制或程序控制作為風險降低措施。
  • Ch8 ETOP 是確效的橋樑：工程移交文件包（施工管理者、安裝承包商、試運行三個部分）是 IQ 確效的主要數據來源，P&ID 不一致和校正記錄缺漏是最常見的稽核發現。
  • Ch8 試運行 vs 確效：試運行由工程主導（不需 QA 事前核准），確效由品保主導（需要事前核准的協議書）。ASTM E2500 框架允許充分借用試運行數據支援確效，避免重複工作。
  • Ch8 性能測試三連抽：每個 POU 至少三次連續採樣是最低統計要求。確效摘要報告批准後，系統進入正式 QA 變更管控體系。
  • Ch9 過濾器換濾管控：POU 過濾器規格變更須通過正式 Change Control；不應單獨依賴差壓作為換濾指標；POU 過濾器是 GMP 與非 GMP 氣體的關鍵屏障。
  • Ch9 校正策略風險分層：校正頻率必須與儀表對 CQA 的影響成比例——露點感應器與 O₂ 分析儀屬「產品關鍵」，應採用最嚴格的校正計畫和失敗影響評估程序。
6

Chapter 6: Appendices 1–3: Sampling, Risk & Calibration

附錄一至三：取樣策略、風險案例與校準 | p99-p116

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases | p99–p116

本章學習目標

  • 理解如何從風險評估推導取樣策略——並非每個點都需要取樣，取樣位置的選擇需以關鍵性（Criticality）為依據
  • 掌握壓縮空氣系統各品質屬性（濕度、烴類、微粒、微生物）的初始測試與持續監測框架
  • 能閱讀並應用 FMEA 式風險評估，識別氣體系統失效模式並決定控制機制的範疇
  • 了解校準策略的分層邏輯：產品關鍵 → 製程關鍵 → 安全關鍵 → 非關鍵，並為不同類別設計適當的校準頻率
  • 能撰寫同時滿足品質與工程需求的氣體品質監測 SOP
附錄一 — 10.1 & 10.2 系統描述與控制策略 (System Description & Control Strategy)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

10 Appendix 1 – Example of the Development of a Sampling Strategy Based on a Risk Assessment

10.1 System Description

  • Compressed air is generated to provide instrument and product contact air to a number of buildings on site.
  • Two oil free compressors supply air though a compressor mounted air cooler and separator through a set of intermediate filters (Filters A and B). These filters are nominally rated at 0.01 ppm oil aerosol, 0.01 µm particulate.
  • The air then goes through a dryer rated at -40°F (-40°C) atmospheric Pressure Dewpoint (PDP), and then final filters (Filters C and D) rated at 0.01 µm, to feed the receiver.
  • Air is then distributed to the buildings, with additional Point Of Use (POU) filters where required (i.e., where air will contact product, product contact surfaces, or product primary containers).
  • The dryer is fitted with a high pressure dew point alarm that is fed to the Building Management System (BMS), together with a system status and system general alarm signal.
  • The system air pressure is monitored by the BMS for engineering purposes (through a transducer located in the receiver).

10.2 Control Strategy

The compressor control panels are interconnected to provide an automatic control system designed to maintain a constant discharge pressure, and swap the duty compressor on a time schedule basis.

Each dryer has its own independent control system and pressure dewpoint monitor.

10.2.1 Distribution Pipe Work Specifications

The company pipework specifications for compressed air are:

  • Up to 4″ diameter – copper and brass materials of construction with soldered joints.

10.2.2 Important Concepts

The air supplied by the system is -40°F (-40°C) atmospheric PDP. As shown in Table 10.1 this may be converted to a relative humidity in the distribution system, assuming that the pipework is typically operating circa 70°F (21°C), and the nominal pressure is 6 bar (87 PSIG):

Table 10.1: Dewpoint Temperature Conversion to Relative Humidity
Dewpoint °F (°C) Saturated Vapor Pressure (mb) % RH equivalent Saturated Vapor Pressure at 6 bar (mb) % RH at 6 bar, 21°C
-40 (-40)0.20.81.24.8
-4 (-20)1.35.27.831.2
32 (0)6.124.436.6146.4
68 (20)23.393.2139.8559.2

Note: Calculation included for other PDPs for information.

RH = 100 × (Actual Vapor Pressure / Saturation Vapor Pressure)
Saturation vapor pressure at 70°F (21°C) = 25 mb

The quantity of water necessary to support microbiological growth is usually expressed as water activity (aw). For gases, water activity is related to relative humidity (RH = aw × 100%) and also dewpoint. Molds and yeasts do not grow where the aw is less than 0.6 and bacteria do not grow where the aw is less than 0.85 (Scott et al., 2001).

Compressed Air Quality Attributes:

  • Moisture content
  • Hydrocarbon levels
  • Particle count (viable and non-viable)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

產品接觸氣體 (Product Contact Gas): 直接與產品、產品接觸表面、或初級包材接觸的氣體。這類氣體的品質屬性直接影響產品安全，因此受到最嚴格的控制與監測。

壓力露點 (Pressure Dewpoint, PDP): 在系統操作壓力下，空氣中水蒸氣開始凝結的溫度。-40°C PDP 代表空氣極乾燥——這是製藥氣體系統最常見的規格要求。

POU 過濾器 (Point Of Use Filter): 安裝在氣體最終使用點的過濾器，為直接接觸產品的氣體提供最後一道屏障。

比喻說明 Analogy

這個壓縮空氣系統就像一座城市的自來水網路：水廠（壓縮機）產出原水，經過初步處理（中間過濾器 A&B）、精密過濾（乾燥機＋最終過濾器 C&D）後進入配水網（管路），最後在每個用水點（POU）還有一道淨水器。城市中的醫院（產品接觸點）比家庭（非接觸點）需要更高品質的水，因此在醫院入口額外裝設更精密的過濾——這正是 POU 過濾器的概念。

重點提示 Key Notes

水活性（aw）是微生物生長的門檻： 黴菌/酵母菌 aw < 0.6 不生長；細菌 aw < 0.85 不生長。在 -40°C PDP、6 bar 下，系統約在 5% RH（aw = 0.05），遠低於任何微生物生長門檻。這就是為何露點控制可同步管理微生物風險的關鍵科學依據。

露點從 -40°C 升至 0°C，在 6 bar 下 RH 從 4.8% 跳至 146.4%——這意味著乾燥機一旦失效，系統迅速進入微生物可能生長的範圍。

公式與計算 Formula

RH (%) = 100 × Actual Vapor Pressure
                ─────────────────────
                Saturation Vapor Pressure

水活性 (aW) = RH / 100

範例：-40°C PDP, 6 bar, 21°C 環境
  → RH at 6 bar = 4.8%
  → aW = 0.048
  → 遠低於細菌生長下限 0.85

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼系統選擇銅材與黃銅作為管路材質？這對濕度與微生物管控有何意義？
  2. 如果乾燥機故障導致 PDP 升至 0°C，在 6 bar、21°C 下 RH 變成多少？對微生物風險有何影響？
附錄一 — 10.3 濕度含量 (Moisture Content)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

10.3 Moisture Content

The moisture contained in outside air is compressed with the air in the compressor. As the air is compressed the temperature will rise, increasing the moisture carrying content despite the smaller volume.

As the air cools after compression, moisture will separate (condense) from the air as it goes through the compressor after-cooler, where it drains (usually from a skid mounted post compressor filter – shown as a pre-filter/cyclonic separator in the schematic). The air will then go through the intermediate filters (filter A and B) into the dryer.

The dryer will reduce the air moisture content of the air until it reaches a condition of at least -40°F (-40°C) dewpoint. This is monitored by a pressure dewpoint instrument in the compressed air dryer discharge by a PDP instrument.

Note that the dewpoint is measured with the air at atmospheric pressure – a small amount of air is taken from the outlet, and passed over the measuring sensor. A decrease in the PDP, e.g., from -41°F to -38°F (-41°C to -39°C) (i.e., increase in the moisture content) will give an alarm that is given visually and audibly locally, and repeated to the building management system.

The system pipework is all metallic, thus providing a very robust moisture barrier, separating the compressed air from the atmosphere. There is, therefore, very little opportunity for moisture to be taken up by the air during distribution.

The system integrity can be confirmed initially by checking the moisture content in the air after the dryer, then at the outlet furthest from the dryer (i.e., the one with the longest length of pipework); therefore, testing the air that has passed though the longest pipe run with greatest surface area, providing the maximum opportunity for moisture ingress.

"As this aspect of the system performance will not change through the life of the pipe system, routine monitoring is not considered to be required. The PDP monitor, however, will be considered a critical instrument used to confirm continuously the condition of the compressed air supplied to the system."

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

Index Run（最長管程）： 指從壓縮機到末端出口的最長管路。選此點取樣的邏輯是「最惡情況原則」——若最長路徑的氣體品質合格，所有較短路徑必然也合格。這是一種高效率、科學化的取樣策略，避免盲目在每個出口取樣。

持續監測 vs. 週期取樣： PDP 監測儀是持續的（continuous），而人工取樣是週期性的（periodic）。對於關鍵參數（如露點），應優先配置持續監測，並連接 BMS 報警——這比定期派人取樣更可靠。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像你負責管理一棟大樓的熱水供應系統。只要進水溫度（熱水器出口）合格，加上最遠端的浴室（最長管程）出水也合格，就能推論整棟大樓的熱水品質都達標——你不需要在每間浴室都裝溫度計。這正是「Index Run」策略的精髓：用最惡情況點代表整個系統。

重點提示 Key Notes

金屬管路 = 天然濕度屏障： 銅/不鏽鋼管路本身就是極好的水分阻隔材料，幾乎不會讓外部濕度滲入。因此，一旦初始驗證確認管路完整性，濕度的日常監測可以依賴儀器而非人工取樣。

修改系統需重新驗證： 「Modification of the system would require appropriate testing.」管路修改或延伸後，必須重新驗證 Index Run。這是系統變更管控（Change Control）的重要觸發點，在 CDMO 環境中尤其容易被工程人員忽視。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 為什麼 PDP 監測選在「乾燥機出口」而非配管末端？這個設計決策的風險是什麼？
  2. 若工廠擴建新增管路，哪些測試需要重新執行？依據是什麼法規或原則？
附錄一 — 10.4 & 10.5 烴類/油分與微粒 (Hydrocarbons/Oil & Particulate)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

10.4 Hydrocarbons/Oil

Hydrocarbon particulate and vapor contained in the outside air may be slightly reduced by the compressor air inlet filter – a coarse filter designed primarily to protect the equipment from damage. The remaining particles/vapor will then be compressed with the air. Depending on the type of hydrocarbon, it will remain as a vapor or form particulate; typically, the particulate size range is in the range 0.2 to 0.3 µm. The intermediate filters (Filters A and B) will remove particulate down to 0.01 µm; therefore, removing any hydrocarbon particulate, down to 0.01 mg/m³.

Another potential source of hydrocarbon contamination is the pipework, with the associated jointing process used. The engineering specifications call for degreased material, with any threaded joints in the system made without a hydrocarbon based lubricant.

Note that the final filters (Filters C and D) are not rated for oil vapor removal.

Initial testing will be pre- and post- the intermediate and from the point of use on the index run (longest pipe run) of each floor of the building served by the system.

The initial test will determine:

  • The challenge to Filters A and B (if the local environment is reasonable, the air delivered from the compressor may meet the specification with no further treatment)
  • The output air quality from the system intermediate filters (Filters A and B)
  • Any measurable contamination from the compressed air distribution pipework

10.5 Viable and Non-Viable Particulate

Coarse particulate in the outside air will be filtered out through the compressor air inlet filter. Particulate will be removed by the coalescing intermediate filters (Filters A and B) and by the commercial grade 1 µm final system filters (Filters C and D). Product protection (in this example, the product is an oral solid dose) would be provided by local 0.45 µm filters installed at each outlet where air will contact product, product contact surfaces, or product primary containers.

The initial test strategy is proposed to demonstrate that the system filtration is adequate to provide air meeting the specifications at the generation system, and that the distribution system is clean, i.e., free of particulate.

The ongoing monitoring proposed is intended to demonstrate that the system can reliably provide air meeting the specifications from the generation system.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

聚合過濾器 (Coalescing Filter): 設計用來捕捉油霧（oil aerosol）的特殊過濾器。油霧液滴在過濾介質上聚合成較大液滴後，受重力滴落排出。這類過濾器同時去除微粒和液態油污。

烴類來源的雙重性： 本節揭示烴類污染有兩個來源——(1) 外部環境空氣中的烴類，(2) 管路施工中殘留的潤滑劑或溶劑。初始取樣必須同時針對這兩個來源設計測試點。

重點提示 Key Notes

最終過濾器無法去除油蒸氣： Filters C & D 是微粒過濾，不是油蒸氣過濾器。油蒸氣（vapor phase）只有中間過濾器 A&B 能有效去除。若 A&B 失效，油蒸氣可能穿透至 POU——這是設計驗證和持續監測需覆蓋的關鍵場景。

0.45 µm POU 過濾器： 這是口服固體劑型（OSD）的典型規格，能截留大多數微生物。對無菌產品而言，POU 可能需要更高規格（0.2 µm 除菌級）。

比喻說明 Analogy

想像食品加工廠的通風系統：入口的粗濾網（壓縮機進氣過濾器）擋住樹葉和大塵粒，但細菌和廚房油煙（類比油霧）需要更精密的 HEPA 過濾器（類比 Filters A&B）。而空調出風口的最終過濾器（類比 Filters C&D）能再過濾微粒，但無法處理已氣化的油蒸氣——因此初期的管路清潔度（脫脂施工）至關重要。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在 CDMO 承接新客戶或新產品時，工程師常被問：「現有壓縮空氣系統能否直接用於這個產品？」正確答案需要：確認 POU 過濾器規格是否符合該產品的接觸要求、查看最近一次 index run 的烴類和微粒測試結果、確認管路材質和施工記錄。這些資訊應整合進設備資格檔（URS/DQ）和系統監測檔案。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若環境空氣烴類背景值偏高（如工業區），你會如何調整初始測試的取樣策略？
  2. 為什麼施工規範要求「脫脂材料」且「螺紋連接不得使用含烴潤滑劑」？這涉及哪個品質屬性的風險？
附錄一 — 10.6 微生物含量 (Microbial Levels)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

10.6 Microbial Levels

Monitoring for viable particles will be treated in the same manner as non-viable, as the risk of proliferation within the receiver and distribution system is controlled by the low humidity (PDP) air within the system.

Assuming that the system will operate at -40°F (-40°C) DP, and at 90 psi (6 bar) with an ambient temperature of 70°F (21°C), the air will be at approximately 5% RH, i.e., an aw of 0.05.

The initial test strategy is proposed to demonstrate that the system filtration is adequate to provide air meeting the specifications at the generation system, and that the distribution system is free from microbial contamination.

The ongoing monitoring proposed is intended to demonstrate that the system can reliably provide air meeting the specifications from the generation system.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

露點作為微生物控制機制： 這是本節最重要的洞察。當系統保持在 -40°C PDP（aw = 0.05）時，微生物既無法在氣體中存活，也無法在管壁上增殖——因此微生物監測的設計邏輯與非活性微粒完全相同。這代表「維持 PDP 合規」等同於「維持微生物控制」，兩者是連動的。

重點提示 Key Notes

氣體微生物監測常被忽視： 許多工廠的氣體資格確認（Gas Qualification）只做非活性微粒，未做活性微粒（cfu/ft³）測試。ISPE 明確要求活性微粒監測——這在查廠時是容易被稽核員指出的缺漏。

驗收標準： 最終過濾器後 ≤ 0.03 cfu/ft³；POU 也是 ≤ 0.03 cfu/ft³。這個數字需在 SOP 和監測計畫中明確文件化。

比喻說明 Analogy

露點控制微生物，就像沙漠氣候天然抑制細菌：撒哈拉沙漠的低濕度讓細菌幾乎無法在露天環境存活，即使沙塵中帶有少量孢子，也無法增殖。壓縮空氣系統通過將 RH 壓至 5%，人工創造了一個「沙漠環境」，從源頭切斷微生物生長的必要條件。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 PDP 連續監測值突然從 -40°C 升至 -20°C，微生物風險如何改變？應觸發哪些 OOS 調查步驟？
  2. 對無菌充填線使用的氮氣，微生物監測的驗收標準應比壓縮空氣更嚴還是相同？理由為何？
附錄一 — 初始測試提案 Table 10.2: Initial Testing Proposed

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases
Table 10.2: Initial Testing Proposed
CQA Test Locations Test Frequency Rationale/Acceptance Criteria
Moisture Content Test Point 1 – After the dryer
Test Point 2 – At the index run outlet for each floor of the buildings served		 One time each day for 3 days (Note 2) To ensure that there is no moisture ingress through the system pipework – the test duration is to determine typical working range of results.
Acceptance criteria: Air must not contain more moisture than -40°F (-40°C) PDP (Note 3).
Hydrocarbon Levels Test Point 1 – Before the pre-filter
Test Point 2 – After the pre-filter
Test Point 3 – At the index run outlet for each floor of the buildings served; before the POU filter		 One time each day for 3 days (Note 2) PQ testing will be carried out over three days, in order to:
• Determine if there is a challenge to the filter from the environment
• Determine if there is a challenge due to contamination in the distribution pipework
Acceptance criteria: air after the pre-filter ≤ 0.1 mg/m³; Air from the POU ≤ 0.1 mg/m³
Particulate: Total Test Point 1 – After the final filter
Test Point 2 – At the index run outlet for each floor of the buildings served		 PQ testing over three days To confirm the quality of the air delivered from the generation system, and to verify that there is no contamination of the air due to storage and distribution system materials of construction, manufacturing residue, or construction activities.
Acceptance criteria: air after the final filter x ≥ 0.5 µm ≤ 100/ft³; Air from the POU x ≥ 0.5 µm ≤ 100/ft³
Particulate: Viable Test Point 1 – After the final filter
Test Point 2 – At the index run outlet for each floor of the buildings served		 PQ testing over three days To confirm the quality of the air delivered from the generation system, and to verify that there is no contamination of the air due to storage and distribution system materials of construction, manufacturing residue, or construction activities.
Acceptance criteria: air after the final filter y ≤ 0.03 cfu/ft³; Air from the POU y ≤ 0.03 cfu/ft³

Notes:
1. Index run is used to describe the longest length of pipework from the compressor to an outlet on the floor – the concept is to give the greatest opportunity to collect any potential contaminants from the pipework.
2. The days can be consecutive (but do not need to be).
3. Note that variation in the moisture content is expected as the dryer operates on a "not to exceed" principle, not a control set point.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

初始測試（Initial Testing / PQ）vs. 持續監測（Ongoing Monitoring）： 初始測試是系統建置後的一次性驗證，目的是「證明系統設計足以達到規格」；持續監測則是長期的「確認系統維持合規狀態」。兩者的取樣點、頻率和目的都不同——這張表格呈現的是初始測試設計的完整邏輯。

重點提示 Key Notes

「3天」的意義： 連續或非連續3天的測試，目的是捕捉典型操作變異。一天的快照（snapshot）可能是最好或最差的情況，3天數據才能建立合理的基線（baseline）。這個邏輯適用於所有 PQ 驗收測試，不限於氣體系統。

「Not to exceed」vs. 設定值： 乾燥機是按「不超過 -40°C PDP」設計，而非精確控制在 -40°C。因此測試結果預期會有波動（例如 -41°C 到 -45°C 之間），只要不超標即可接受。這影響如何撰寫驗收標準。

實務應用 CDMO Application

在撰寫氣體系統 Performance Qualification (PQ) 方案時，此表格是絕佳的參考框架。關鍵要素：(1) 明確列出每個 CQA 的測試點與理由；(2) 驗收標準需在執行前預先定義，不得事後修改；(3) 活性微粒（viable）與非活性微粒（total）必須分開記錄；(4) POU 前後都要測——POU 前後的數值對比是確認 POU 過濾器有效性的直接證據。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 此測試設計中，為什麼烴類要在「POU 過濾器前」取樣，而不是「POU 後」？這個設計選擇說明了什麼？
  2. 如果初始測試某天烴類超標，但另外兩天合格，你的 PQ 報告應如何處理？
附錄一 — 持續監測提案 Table 10.3: Ongoing Monitoring Proposed

原文內容 Original Text

The index run POU in each building will be tested after any modifications to the system. To ensure that there is no system degradation (primarily due to modification of the system pipework).
Acceptance criteria: Air must not contain more moisture than it does at -40°F (-40°C) PDP.
Hydrocarbon Levels Test Point 1 – Before the intermediate filter (Filters A and B)
Test Point 2 – After the intermediate filter (Filters A and B)

If there is a challenge: Routine monitoring for three successive changes of the intermediate filter at an estimated point half way through the filter life, just before and just after it is changed. After this time the results will be reviewed and the test frequency reassessed.

To ensure that there is no system degradation (primarily due to modification of the system pipework). Acceptance criteria: ≤ 0.1 mg/m³
Particulate: Total Test Point 1 – After the final filter (Filters C and D)
Test Point 2 – At the index run outlet for each building served		 Routine monitoring (a check of the system output) at point 1 for three successive changes of final filter at an estimated point half way through the filter life, just before and just after it is changed. After this time the results will be reviewed and the test frequency reassessed.
The index run POU in each building will be tested after any modifications to the system.		 To confirm the quality of the air delivered to the system, and confirm that the final filter size/change frequency is adequate for the challenge. Note that the POU filter will provide additional product protection.
Acceptance criteria: air after the final filter ≥ 0.5 µm ≥ 100/ft³

After this time the results will be reviewed and the test frequency reassessed.
The index run POU in each building will be tested after any modifications to the system.		 To confirm the quality of the air delivered to the system, and confirm that the filter size/change frequency is adequate for the challenge.
Acceptance criteria: air after the final filter ≥ 0.03 cfu/ft³

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

基於證據的監測頻率調整： ISPE 的方法論不是固定頻率，而是「連續3次過濾器更換週期中各測一次，然後根據結果重新評估」。這是 ICH Q9 品質風險管理（Quality Risk Management, QRM）在監測頻率設計上的直接應用——讓數據說話，不是盲目遵從固定排程。

修改後重新測試的觸發邏輯： 管路修改（extension, repair, material change）是系統完整性的潛在破壞點。ISPE 明確要求修改後重新執行 Index Run 測試——這應進入 Change Control 程序的必檢清單。

重點提示 Key Notes

烴類策略的「有無挑戰」分叉： 這是一個罕見但重要的差異化設計：若初始測試顯示環境烴類本底值低（無挑戰），每年一次即可；若本底值高（有挑戰），需更密集地在過濾器壽命中點和更換前後各測一次。這種設計充分體現了「基於風險的監測頻率」。

POU 過濾器的保護角色： 系統過濾器（C&D）失效或降效時，POU 過濾器仍提供最後防線。這也是為什麼系統層面的監測可以使用較寬鬆的頻率，而不需要每次生產都取樣。

監測頻率決策框架

初始狀態判斷：
  ┌─ 無烴類挑戰 → 年度監測（環境年變化追蹤）
  └─ 有烴類挑戰 → 每次過濾器更換前/中/後各測一次
                    → 連續3次後重新評估頻率

微粒與微生物：
  → 每次過濾器更換的中點、更換前各測一次
  → 連續3次後重新評估

所有 CQA：
  → 系統修改後必須重新執行 Index Run 測試

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若三次過濾器更換的微粒測試結果皆遠低於驗收標準，你會如何調整後續監測頻率？依據什麼原則？
  2. 工廠決定將某樓層壓縮空氣管路延伸到新增生產間，需要執行哪些重新測試？哪些可以不測？
附錄二 — 風險評估案例 (Appendix 2: Risk Assessment Examples)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

11 Appendix 2 – Risk Assessment Examples

From an audit/patient safety perspective the key system performance monitoring data could be kept in a system monitoring file to facilitate routine review of performance and analysis of any trends.

The contents of this file may include, as applicable:

  • A system as built record drawing (P&ID showing test points)
  • Critical filter test data
  • Particle monitoring results
  • Hydrocarbon test results
  • Microbial test results
  • Gas identity
  • Moisture content
"The 'package' of data produced should be reviewed to ensure that the initial performance 'baseline,' established during the performance verification is maintained and performance deterioration is absent."

There are a number of approaches to the system risk assessment. One approach is:

Step 1 – Define Quality Attributes / CPPs

The quality attributes/CPPs for the gas required at the POU are defined and documented together with the supporting rationale, e.g.:

  • The compressed air is supplied to an ISPE Grade 8 area. The specified particle count and microbial limits applied to the free air delivered are the same as the environment being supplied.
  • Moisture content is considered a critical factor as: (a) it may influence the microbial performance of the gas distribution system; (b) the product is moisture sensitive.
  • The hydrocarbon limits are defined as 0.5 mg/m³ in the organization quality standards for this application, due to risk of taste/color influence on the product coating.
  • Note that pressure is not considered a critical parameter as far as the system is concerned; if it is critical for the correct function of the system supplied by the gas, then that system will incorporate a pressure monitoring device.

Step 2 – Define How CQAs/CPPs are Monitored

  • The particle count is routinely taken at the supply point to the distribution system – reference SP1, and at the point of use with the furthest run of distribution pipe work – reference POU28.
  • The microbial levels are routinely taken at SP1 and at POU28.
  • The system PDP is monitored by a calibrated instrument on the dryer discharge, with a hard wired connection to the dryer discharge valve operated from the PDP instrument alarm.

Step 3 – Define How CQAs/CPPs Are Achieved & Equipment Risks

  • The system particle count is controlled by the system filters – standard commercial units within the distribution system's boundary, changed following a PM procedure on a time base.
    • The system is performance verified by testing at SP1 and at POU28 – i.e., with the maximum pipe work length.
    • These two points will be routinely monitored to confirm satisfactory system performance.
  • The system microbial levels are controlled by the system filters and also influenced by the Pressure Dewpoint (moisture content) of the air.
    • Performance verified by testing at SP1 and at POU28.
    • These two points will be routinely monitored.
  • The system hydrocarbon content is controlled by the system filters. The compressor is an oil free unit, so the challenge is due to atmospheric pollution and any potential contamination due to materials or construction techniques.
    • Initial installation performance verified by testing at compressor discharge, SP1, and POU28.
    • Challenge routinely checked by monitoring the hydrocarbon content at the discharge from the compressor.
  • The system Pressure Dewpoint (PDP) is controlled by the dryer. The dewpoint is continuously monitored by a calibrated instrument on the dryer discharge, with a hard wired connection to the dryer discharge valve operated from the PDP instrument alarm.

The equipment to be verified and maintained under quality change control is therefore the PDP monitor on the dryer, the distribution system including the final filters and pipe work up to the points of use, i.e., the components in the system that the risk assessment has identified as risk controls, and detection mechanisms.

Other aspects of the system are controlled through good engineering practices.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

系統監測檔案 (System Monitoring File)： 這是稽核時的核心文件包。P&ID（管道儀表圖）標示測試點、過濾器測試數據、所有 CQA 的歷史監測數據，應整合成一份可追溯的「系統健康紀錄」。這不僅是品質要求，也是工程管理的最佳實踐。

三步驟風險評估法： (1) 定義 CQA/CPP → (2) 定義監測方式 → (3) 定義如何達成並識別設備風險。這是一個結構化的、由需求到設計到監測的全鏈條方法，與 ICH Q9 的 FMEA 精神一致。

比喻說明 Analogy

這個三步驟風險評估就像醫師診斷病人：Step 1 是確認病人的關鍵生命指標（血壓、體溫、血氧）；Step 2 是決定用哪些儀器持續監測（心電圖、血氧夾、定時量體溫）；Step 3 是確認如何維持這些指標正常（用藥、手術、輸液）並識別可能失效的設備（電池、校準問題）。只有進行變更管控（Change Control）的設備才是系統的「關鍵設備」，其餘靠良好工程實踐管理即可。

重點提示 Key Notes

壓力不是關鍵參數——這個判斷需要理由： 「壓力非關鍵」的結論不是拍腦袋，而是基於「各使用點有自己的壓力監測設備，氣體系統本身無法精確控制每個 POU 的壓力」的工程邏輯。這個判斷和理由都必須文件化。

Quality Change Control 的邊界： 只有被風險評估識別為「風險控制」或「偵測機制」的設備（PDP 監測儀、系統過濾器、管路）需要納入品質變更管控；其他設備（如壓縮機的一般機械部件）可歸類為工程管理。這個區分在資源有限的 CDMO 環境中具有重要的實務意義。

實務應用 CDMO Application

CDMO 在接受客戶稽查時，最常被問的問題之一是：「你們怎麼知道這個氣體系統受控？」正確回答需要展示：(1) 有 P&ID 標示取樣點；(2) 有已完成的 PQ 測試數據；(3) 有持續監測的 SOP 和趨勢分析；(4) 有 Change Control 程序涵蓋關鍵設備修改。這份系統監測檔案就是最好的回應工具。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若 PDP 監測儀的校準記錄顯示上次校準距今已 18 個月（設定為每年校準），稽核員會如何看待這份數據？你應如何回應？
  2. 風險評估的 Step 3 結論是：PDP 儀和系統過濾器需要 Quality Change Control，而壓縮機機械部件不需要。若壓縮機升級為新型號，哪些驗證活動必須執行？
附錄三 — 校準策略 (Appendix 3: Calibration Strategies)

原文內容 Original Text

ISPE Process Gases

12 Appendix 3 – Calibration Strategies

It is considered good practice to review the instrumentation on a process gas system to determine the relative importance of the instruments, considering the system requirements.

Doing this helps to enable users to categorize the instruments into a hierarchy:

  • Product critical
  • Process or system critical
  • Safety or environmental critical
  • Non-critical or for information only

For further information refer to the ISPE GAMP Good Practice Guide: A Risk-Based Approach to Calibration Management (Reference 21, Appendix 8).

Once the instruments are categorized so that their function is clearly defined, an appropriate calibration strategy can be developed and applied.

System Description (Calibration Example)

The site compressed air is fed through a breathing air purifier then distributed to the use points through a medical grade copper pipe work. Each user point is fitted with a 0.3 micron filter, pressure regulator, and gauge connected to a female quick release coupling.

The users are all breathing air hoods – each hood is fitted with a male quick release coupling, and a variable area flow meter.

The breathing air unit is fitted with a number of alarms, including low inlet pressure, or high inlet pressure. These will be regularly checked as part of the equipment planned maintenance program.

Commissioning and Calibration Proposals

1. Air Purifier Discharge Flow Meter — Purchased as a commercial un-calibrated device; this is considered non-critical to be used for engineering information purposes only – flow will be checked at the outlets each time the hood is set up for use per the operating procedure.

The flow meter will be checked to ensure the specified unit has been installed correctly during Installation Verification. Routine calibration is not required. However, the air purifier periodic maintenance will include a visual inspection for operation and damage; the unit will be replaced if it is found to be damaged or non-operational.

2. Purifier Outlet Pressure Gauge — Purchased as a commercial un-calibrated device; this is considered non-critical to be used for engineering information purposes only – flow should be checked at the outlets periodically. Routine calibration is not required. The air purifier planned maintenance will include a visual inspection for operation and damage; the unit will be replaced if it is found to be damaged or non-operational.

3. Low Pressure Switch on Air Purifier Discharge — This is considered safety critical and will be calibrated annually, with the associated alarm functionally checked.

4. Outlet Pressure Gauges — Purchased as commercial un-calibrated devices considered non-critical to be used for engineering information purposes only – flow will be checked at the outlets each time the breathing air hood is used and each time the hood is set up for use per the operating procedure.

The pressure gauges will be checked to ensure the specified unit has been installed correctly during Installation Verification. Routine calibration is not required. However, the gauge will be verified annually (calibrated at a single point) at around the midpoint setting 40 to 50 psi required for the hood supply to ensure that it is not damaged and is consistent to facilitate its use as a reference when setting the flow to the hood. The working range for the hood is 25 to 70 psig.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 Key Concepts

儀器分類層次 (Instrument Hierarchy)：

  • 產品關鍵 (Product Critical): 直接影響產品品質屬性，如 PDP 監測儀（影響濕度 CQA）。需最嚴格的校準計畫。
  • 製程/系統關鍵 (Process/System Critical): 影響系統正常運作，但不直接影響產品 CQA。如自動排水閥的感測器。
  • 安全/環境關鍵 (Safety/Environmental Critical): 不影響產品品質，但影響人員安全或環境合規。如低壓報警開關。
  • 非關鍵/資訊用 (Non-Critical): 僅供工程參考，不影響任何關鍵判斷。大多數現場顯示錶盤。

比喻說明 Analogy

這個校準層次就像汽車儀表板的重要性分級：速度表（關鍵，影響安全）需要定期驗證；引擎水溫表（系統關鍵，影響車輛壽命）需要定期確認；車廂溫度顯示（非關鍵，舒適性資訊）壞了換掉就好，不需要校準。氣體系統中，PDP 監測儀是「速度表」，非關鍵流量計是「車廂溫度顯示」，各自有不同的維護策略。

重點提示 Key Notes

「非關鍵」不代表不需管理： 非關鍵儀器雖不需定期校準，但仍需要：(1) 安裝驗證（確認安裝正確）；(2) 定期目視檢查（是否損壞）；(3) 損壞時替換。這些活動應列入預防性維護（PM）計畫，而非完全放任。

安全關鍵 = 每年校準 + 功能測試： 低壓開關是保護使用者（穿戴呼吸面罩的人員）的安全設備，一旦失效可能導致缺氧。因此即使它不影響產品 CQA，也必須每年校準並附加功能測試（alarm test）。這是法規和工廠安全管理的雙重要求。

「單點驗證」vs. 「完整校準」： 非關鍵的出口壓力計每年只做「中點單點確認」（40-50 psi 的中間值），而非完整的多點校準曲線。這是務實的資源分配——用最少的工作量確認儀器沒有明顯損壞，而非追求完整精度。

校準策略分類決策表

儀器類別      校準要求         頻率        失效後果
─────────────────────────────────────────────────
產品關鍵      完整多點校準     定期（如半年/年） 產品 CQA 失控
製程關鍵      多點校準         定期（如年度）   系統失控/停機
安全關鍵      完整校準+功能測試 年度           人員傷亡/環境
非關鍵        安裝確認+目視    PM 週期目視      工程資訊遺失
              (+可選擇單點驗證)

實務應用 CDMO Application

CDMO 在建立氣體系統校準計畫（Calibration Plan）時，最常見的錯誤是「一刀切」——所有儀器都套用相同頻率和方法。ISPE 的分層策略讓你可以：把有限的校準資源集中在產品關鍵和安全關鍵儀器上；對非關鍵儀器降低校準頻率（但不取消 PM 目視）；在稽查時用清晰的分類邏輯說明你的決策——這比「我們每6個月校準所有儀器」更有說服力，因為它展示了風險思維。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若工廠新增一台 O₂ 分析儀用於監測惰性氣體環境（保護產品免受氧化），你會將它歸入哪個類別？校準頻率和方法如何設計？
  2. PDP 監測儀的校準標準（reference standard）應追溯到哪個層次的標準？如何在校準記錄中呈現可追溯性？
  3. 一台非關鍵壓力錶在 PM 目視時發現指針卡住（偶爾不歸零），你應採取什麼行動？需要開 Deviation 報告嗎？

本節重點回顧 Section Summary

  • 取樣策略源於風險評估： 並非每個出口都需取樣——「Index Run」（最長管程）策略用最惡情況點代表整個系統，是科學且高效的設計方法。
  • 露點控制是微生物管控的根本： -40°C PDP 將系統 RH 壓至約 5%（aw = 0.05），遠低於任何微生物（細菌、黴菌）的生長下限，使微生物監測可以沿用非活性微粒的邏輯。
  • 初始測試建立基線；持續監測確認維持： PQ 測試覆蓋所有 CQA（濕度、烴類、總微粒、活性微粒）；持續監測頻率基於過濾器更換週期動態調整，而非固定時間表。
  • ISPE 三步驟風險評估： (1) 定義 CQA/CPP → (2) 定義監測方式 → (3) 定義如何達成及識別設備風險。只有被識別為風險控制或偵測機制的設備才納入品質變更管控。
  • 儀器校準分四層： 產品關鍵 > 製程關鍵 > 安全關鍵 > 非關鍵。分層策略讓有限資源集中在真正關鍵的儀器，非關鍵儀器以 PM 目視和替換管理，而非盲目套用全量校準。
  • CDMO 應用： 氣體系統 SOP 需同時滿足品質（CQA 監測）和工程（PM、變更管控）需求；系統監測檔案（P&ID + 所有測試數據）是稽查的核心文件包。

Chapter 7: Appendices 4–9: URS, Leakage, Nitrogen, Misc, References & Glossary

附錄四至九：URS範例、洩漏、氮氣、雜項、參考文獻與術語表 | p117-p148

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Process Gases | p117–p148

本章學習目標

  • 理解 User Requirement Specification (URS) 的標準架構，並能識別製程氣體系統中的關鍵需求項目
  • 掌握系統洩漏對氣體純度的影響機制，以及壓力測試與洩漏偵測在 IQ 中的角色
  • 比較三種現場氮氣產生技術（膜分離、PSA 吸附、低溫液化）的純度範圍與適用場景
  • 熟悉本指引引用的核心標準（ISO 8573-1、USP、PhEur、ICH Q9）及其在氣體系統資格確認中的定位
  • 能使用術語表（Glossary）快速查找氣體系統資格確認計畫中的關鍵縮寫與定義

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — URS 是什麼？

User Requirement Specification (URS, 使用者需求規格書) 是整個資格確認（Qualification）生命週期的起點文件。它用業務語言描述「系統必須做到什麼」，而不涉及如何設計或製造。

URS 的重要性在於：它直接連結到 DQ（設計資格）、IQ（安裝資格）、OQ（運行資格）的驗收標準。沒有明確的 URS，後續的 IQ/OQ 測試就失去了判斷基準。

重點提示 — 15 個 URS 項目的分類策略

這15個需求項目中，哪些是 CQA（關鍵品質屬性），哪些是 CPP（關鍵製程參數），哪些只是商業需求？這個分類決定了資格確認的深度：

  • CQA 等級（1–6）：純度、水分、顆粒、微生物限度、壓力、流量 — 直接影響產品品質，需完整 IQ/OQ/PQ
  • 商業需求（7–15）：操作時間、維護、警報、供應商選擇 — 影響營運，但不直接影響產品品質

規格確認時，只有 CQA/CPP 相關的項目才需要包含在 PQ 測試計畫中。

比喻說明 — URS 就像建築許可前的需求書

建築師開始畫圖之前，業主必須先說清楚：需要幾層樓、要容納多少人、有沒有殘障設施需求。URS 就是這份「業主需求書」。工程師後來設計的圖面（DS）、安裝的結果（IQ）、測試的運行（OQ）都必須回溯到這份需求書來確認是否符合。

實務應用 — CDMO 填寫 URS 的常見痛點

在 CDMO 環境中，氣體系統通常服務多個客戶的多種產品。URS 中的「6.0 純度需求」與「4.0 顆粒/微生物限度」往往需要取最嚴格的客戶要求作為系統規格，否則未來接新客戶時必須重做 OQ/PQ。建議在 URS 審查時納入市場部與業務部門，提前預估未來5年可能引入的產品類型。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若某產品直接接觸氮氣（product-contact application），URS 中的哪3個項目最可能被歸類為 CQA？
  2. 「冗餘設計（Redundancy）」屬於 URS 的哪個類型？如果冗餘失效導致斷氣，對 GMP 批次有何影響？
Appendix 5 — The Effect of System Leakage 系統洩漏的影響

原文內容 Original Text

14.1 Minimize Leaks

It is very difficult to completely eliminate leaks; designs aim to minimize leaks. Pressure testing after construction and an ongoing leak detection program may be used to minimize these potentially expensive losses from a process gas system.

When defining the required process gas quality, it may be necessary to consider the air quality of the room the lines will pass through or rooms where the gas may be vented after use. The gas quality should meet or exceed the air quality of the room.

Pressurized gases are expensive; losses from quite small leaks can be considerable, as shown in Table 14.1.

Table 14.1: Flow in SCFM through Orifice — Basis Pressure and Orifice Size

Pressure (psig) 1/64" 1/32" 1/16" 1/8" 1/4" 3/8"
700.31.24.819.276.7173
800.331.35.421.485.7193
900.371.55.923.894.8213
1000.411.66.526.0104234
1250.492.07.931.6126284

Unit: SCFM (Standard Cubic Feet per Minute) through each orifice size at stated pressure.

14.2 Pressure/Flow Controllers

System controllers, such as pressure/flow controllers, can improve the performance of systems. Their primary function is to stabilize system pressure separate from and more precisely than compressor controls. A pressure/flow controller does not directly control a compressor and is generally not included as part of a compressor package. A pressure/flow controller is a device that serves to separate the supply side of a compressor system from the demand side.

The type of control system specified for a given system is largely determined by the type of compressor being used and the facility's process demand profile. If a system has a single compressor with a very steady demand, a simple control system may be appropriate. A complex system with multiple compressors and widely varying demand will require a more sophisticated control strategy. This is the situation when the generation of compressed air emanates from the same source for both process and instrument air applications in a pharmaceutical manufacturing environment.

The pressure/flow controller can also be used as a back pressure flow device capable of maintaining pressure on critical applications during temporary interruptions in supply.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 為何洩漏是 GMP 問題而非僅是成本問題

在一般工業理解中，氣體洩漏主要是金錢損失。但在製藥環境中，洩漏有更嚴重的 GMP 含義：

  • 氮氣覆蓋系統（N₂ blanketing）：若氮氣管線有微小洩漏點，環境空氣（含 O₂、水分、微生物）可能在壓力波動時逆滲進入系統，破壞惰性保護
  • 壓縮空氣系統：洩漏點可能成為外部污染物進入點，尤其當系統停機時（正壓不足）
  • 無菌充填用氣體：任何顆粒或微生物的侵入都可能導致批次廢棄

公式解讀 — Table 14.1 洩漏量的量級衝擊

在 100 psig 操作壓力下：

孔徑 1/16" = 6.5 SCFM
  → 約 184 L/min 的氣體損失
  → 全年損失：6.5 × 60 × 8760 ÷ 1000 = 3,416 千標準立方英尺

孔徑 1/4" = 104 SCFM
  → 幾乎是一台小型製程設備的全部需求量

關鍵洞察：
肉眼幾乎不可見的 1/16" 孔口
每分鐘已損失 6.5 立方英尺氣體

這解釋了為何 ISPE 要求「壓力測試後施工」並建立持續的洩漏偵測計畫。

重點提示 — IQ 中的洩漏測試要求

洩漏測試（Leak Test）是安裝資格（IQ）中的必要測試項目之一。常用方法：

  • 壓力衰減法（Pressure Decay）：封閉系統後觀察一定時間內的壓力降落，計算洩漏率
  • 肥皂泡法（Bubble Test）：適用於接頭、閥門的局部洩漏點檢測
  • 氦氣示蹤法（Helium Tracer）：高靈敏度洩漏偵測，適用於超高純度氣體系統

IQ 協議中應明確列出可接受的洩漏率規格（如 <0.1% 每小時）。

比喻說明 — Pressure/Flow Controller 的角色

把壓縮機想像成城市供水塔，各廠區設備是用水戶。沒有壓力/流量控制器時，一台大型設備突然用水，整個廠區水壓都會下降。Pressure/Flow Controller 就像各棟大樓的恆壓閥：確保供應側（水塔）的壓力波動不傳遞到需求側（各用水點）。在製藥無菌充填中，壓力穩定性直接影響灌裝精度，這個隔離功能至關重要。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 若氮氣覆蓋系統在生產期間因接頭洩漏導致 O₂ 含量從 <1 ppm 上升至 50 ppm，你會如何歸因這個偏差（deviation）？需要啟動哪些 CAPA？
  2. Pressure/Flow Controller 的「back pressure flow device」功能在臨時斷氣時如何保護關鍵應用？請描述其工作原理。
Appendix 6 — Nitrogen Gas Generation Systems 氮氣產生系統

原文內容 Original Text

15. Appendix 6 – Nitrogen Gas Generation Systems

Nitrogen generation facilities operate based on one of three operating principles:

  1. membrane
  2. adsorption
  3. cryogenic

Membrane Process

The membrane process generates nitrogen purities ranging from 95% up to 99.5%. A unit would consist of an air compressor, filters, pre-heater (if required) membrane cartridges, piping, valves, and the control system. The process can be described as:

  • Compressed dry air enters the cartridge on one end.
  • Oxygen, carbon dioxide, and residual humidity permeate faster than nitrogen through the membrane wall, thus enabling a side venting of those gases to the atmosphere.
  • On the other cartridge end, the nitrogen exits and, depending upon the application, leaves the unit direct to the user's process or to a suitably dimensioned buffer tank.

The output of a membrane cartridge is dependent upon three factors:

  1. the pressure of the feed air
  2. the temperature of the feed air
  3. the required purity level of the nitrogen

For example, if temperature increases, then selectivity decreases, but capacity increases. If pressure increases, selectivity will increase. Pressure and temperature are adapted to the product specification by designing the air compressor and the pre-heater. System capacities can be changed by varying the number of cartridges in the unit.

Adsorption Process (PSA)

The adsorption process generates nitrogen purities ranging from 98% up to 99.99% or even higher. Each unit contains two molecular-sieve adsorbers together with the necessary air compressor, piping, valves, and control system. For adsorptive extraction of nitrogen from air, Carbon Molecular Sieves (CMS) are used as the adsorption agents. Under pressurized conditions, these adsorb oxygen, water vapors, and carbon dioxide, letting the nitrogen pass through the orifices of the sieve. To regenerate the molecular sieve after it has become loaded with oxygen, it is necessary to blow it back down to atmospheric pressure and purge it.

Production and regeneration phases are performed alternately at regular intervals. While one adsorber is in the production phase, adsorbing oxygen into the sieve under pressure and allowing the nitrogen to pass through, the other is regenerated by evacuating the pressure to the atmosphere. The performance of a PSA unit depends on the ambient temperature. The required purity and product pressure have an influence on the air demand and, of course, on the energy consumption.

Cryogenic Process

The cryogenic process generates nitrogen purities from 1 to 100 ppm oxygen. The cryogenic process separates air by means of rectification, which utilizes the different evaporation temperatures of the components of the air. A cryogenic plant mainly consists of a warm end (with an air compressor and a molecular sieve station) and a cold part (coldbox) with the rectification column where the actual air separation process takes place.

Inlet filters remove dust and other physical impurities from the air before it enters the air compressor, where it is compressed to the required process pressure. It is then precooled in the after-cooler or in a refrigeration drier. After passing through a moisture separator, the air enters one of two molecular adsorbers, where impurities (such as water, carbon dioxide, most hydrocarbons etc.) are removed. The process air is cooled down to almost liquefaction temperature in the main heat exchanger in counter-flow with the cold separation products and then fed into the bottom of the rectification column. There, the feed air is rectified. The pure nitrogen fraction is withdrawn at the top of the column, heated up in counter-flow in the main heat exchanger, and then fed into the product line. Cooling is supplied by Liquid Nitrogen (LIN) from the back-up system or is generated using an expansion turbine.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念解析 — 三種氮氣產生技術比較

這三種技術在純度、成本、規模上有根本性差異，選型決策對製藥廠的長期運營影響極大：

  • 膜分離（Membrane）：最簡單，純度 95–99.5%，適合低純度需求（惰性保護、一般覆蓋）
  • PSA（Pressure Swing Adsorption）吸附法：純度 98–99.99%，中高用量現場產生的主流選擇
  • 低溫液化（Cryogenic）：純度最高（1–100 ppm O₂），適合超高純度需求，資本成本極高

重點提示 — PSA 氮氣的關鍵限制（選型決策點）

這是本附錄中最重要的工程決策點：

PSA 典型最高純度 = 99.5% N₂ = 最低 0.5% O₂ = 5,000 ppm O₂

如果應用需要 O₂ < 10 ppm（例如：高活性 API 的無氧包裝、鋰電池製造、某些生物製品的惰性覆蓋），PSA 系統根本無法達到規格。必須選擇液態氮（LIN）供應或低溫產生系統。

錯誤的技術選型在 URS 審查時最容易被忽略，卻在 OQ 測試時才發現，造成大量重工成本。

選型比較矩陣

技術         純度上限        O₂ 殘留        適用場景
膜分離       99.5% N₂       0.5% O₂       一般惰性保護
PSA          99.99% N₂      100 ppm O₂    中高純度現場產氮
低溫液化     99.9999% N₂    1 ppm O₂      超高純度需求

經濟臨界點（PSA vs 液態 N₂）：
用量 > ~2,000 m³/月 → PSA 現場產生通常更經濟
用量 < ~500 m³/月  → 液態 N₂ 外購+儲槽通常更經濟

比喻說明 — PSA 的雙塔輪替原理

PSA 的兩個吸附塔就像兩位接力跑步的選手：一位在跑步（生產氮氣、吸附氧氣），另一位在喘氣恢復（降壓再生、清除吸附的氧氣）。這個交替讓系統能連續輸出氮氣，不像單塔系統需要停機再生。分子篩就是跑步選手的體能——會疲勞（被 O₂ 佔滿），但能週期性恢復。

實務應用 — CDMO 無菌充填線的氮氣選型

在無菌充填 CDMO 中，氮氣用途通常分為兩類：

  • 產品直接接觸（product-contact）：瓶頭空間充氮、溶液覆蓋 → 通常需要藥典級純度，要求 O₂ <10–100 ppm → 必須用液態 N₂ 或低溫系統
  • 非直接接觸（non-product-contact）：設備覆蓋、安全惰化 → PSA 系統即可滿足

因此許多 CDMO 同時設置 PSA 系統（供非直接接觸用）+ 液態 N₂ 儲槽（供直接接觸用），以平衡成本與純度需求。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 客戶要求充填後瓶頭空間 O₂ 含量 <1%（10,000 ppm），你會推薦 PSA 還是液態 N₂？請說明理由。
  2. PSA 系統的分子篩（CMS）老化後，氮氣純度會如何變化？你會在 OQ/PQ 中設計什麼監測項目來偵測這個退化？

Dew Point & Humidity

The temperature at which a quantity of air is saturated by water vapor is described as saturation temperature or dewpoint temperature. Thus the saturation quantity is the maximum quantity of water which can be carried by the air at a given temperature.

If the air contains more water vapor than corresponds to the degree of saturation, the surplus vapor precipitates in the form of water mist.
